Commentary

We're Waiting for You on the Front Lines 21

— Zhen

Recently, Army Commander Sun Dianying telegraphed condolences to Division Commander Guan Linzheng from the front lines. There was a most tragic sentence in the telegram: "We are waiting for you on the front lines." How magnificent those words are! We truly hear his voice and see his person.

Yue Wu Mu said it well: "If civil officials do not want money and military officials are not afraid of death, then the world will be at peace." The reason why our country today cannot defend its territory and cannot resist insults is that a large nation with vast land and many people has been turned into a fish on the chopping block, at the mercy of others. Although the reasons for this are diverse, "civil officials wanting money and military officials being afraid of death" is the most important reason. The people provide their blood and sweat to support the army, exceeding two million men. However, with such a huge army, they are only tools for internal warfare. As for the great enemy of our nation, they sit and watch, or even guide the enemy to penetrate deep. How can such irresponsible soldiers not be moved to the core and feel ashamed when they hear Army Commander Sun shouting the tragic cry, "We are waiting for you on the front lines," on the front lines?

In the January 28th Battle of Shanghai, the people of the whole country enthusiastically donated and warmly cared for the soldiers fighting against the Japanese. This time, they also admire and love the soldiers on the front lines outside the passes. Therefore, we believe that under the current circumstances, soldiers have the most opportunities to serve the country and are most likely to win the favor of the people, renewing the people's aversion to soldiers over the past 20 years. If, under such circumstances, the soldiers of the whole country still cannot shoulder the responsibility of saving the country and resisting Japan, then they are truly willing to be the criminals of the nation.

Looking back at history, the demise of every country has been due to civil officials wanting money, making politics as chaotic as tangled silk, and military officials being afraid of death, leaving the country without the power to defend itself. When foreign invaders come, they either watch from the other side of the river or fight on their own. In recent history, the demise of the Ming Dynasty was due to this. However, the current situation in our country is as dangerous as it was at the end of the Ming Dynasty. We are already standing on the line of life and death. If we are unwilling to let our nation perish, now is the last time to awaken and the last time to save the country. Rush to the front lines! There are people on the front lines waving to us. People all along the line are nodding to us. The soldiers of the whole country should rise up and go to the front lines to fight with their blood and flesh. The people of the whole country, in particular, should rise up and do their best to serve the country, uniting their spirit with that of the soldiers on the front lines. This is the only way out for our nation today.

"We are waiting for you on the front lines." This voice is tragic and powerful. We should treat it as a battle drum for a charge, as a bugle call to mobilize the whole nation. Answer with one voice: Coming… Coming!

Japan Is Expanding Its Army 22

Enlisting New Squads of Junior and Non-Commissioned Officers Numbering 100,000

Undergoing Strict Special Training in Gas and Air Warfare

(Tokyo) After the Diet, which adjourned on March 25, passed all military proposals, the Ministry of the Army has now announced procedures for expanding the army, including a provision to form new squads of junior and non-commissioned officers from the active and reserve lists, numbering approximately 100,000 in total. They will undergo special training in gas warfare, the use of armored vehicles, and meteorological testing for military purposes. The procedures also include the establishment of primary aviation training teams, the reorganization of aviation units nationwide, and the creation of nine squadrons of bombers and fighters. In addition, the number of students in the officer academies will be increased to 360, the equipment of military training schools in various locations will be improved, a training school for gas warfare will be established, and military dogs will be trained on a large scale at the Kanto Infantry School. In the past, the conscription system had a provision that paying a certain fee could shorten the term of military service, but this has now been removed. Some lieutenants and second lieutenants on the reserve list will be transferred to the active list, and the number of sergeants on the active list will also be greatly increased. (31st Reuters)

At the Division Commander Meeting, There Was a Chorus of Voices Preparing for Foreign War 23

(Tokyo) On the second day of the Japanese Army Commander and Division Commander Meeting, commanders of related local areas and senior staff members of the General Staff Headquarters attended. The scope of the meeting included General Staff Chief Prince Kan'in's address on national defense deployments, with detailed explanations by Vice Chief of Staff Masaki. Director-General Umezu explained improvements in armaments, reforms in troop organization, and the enrichment of equipment. Director of the First Department Furushō explained modern warfare mobilization, Director of the Second Department Nagata explained the recent situation in China and international relations, and Director of the Third Department Mizumaki explained the military transportation and communication organization. After careful deliberation, the meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM. (31st China United Press)

Plans to Add Airfields for Nationwide Aviation Communication 24

(Tokyo) Following the Japanese government's withdrawal from the League of Nations, relations between Japan and the United States and between Japan and Russia are becoming increasingly complex. The Japanese military, to prepare for any eventuality, is not only adding the latest military airfield in Taiwan in the south, but is also building the latest military airfields in Aomori, Sendai, and Sapporo on the mainland. The main purpose is to link Taiwan in the south, defend Hokkaido in the north, and plan for coordinated aviation communication to provide wartime rescue and transport of military supplies. The cost is set at 1.6 million yen, and it is expected to begin in April and be completed before the Army, Navy, and Air Force's grand maneuvers in August. (31st China United Press)

Preventing Domestic Revolution: Commencing Organization of Voluntary Police Corps 25

(Tokyo) In order to encourage national unity and suppress domestic revolutionary movements after withdrawing from the League of Nations, the Japanese government recently convened a meeting of police chiefs, using the pretext of an emergency situation to plan the expansion and strengthening of the voluntary police officer system. The Police Affairs Bureau has already submitted a standard proposal, ordering all prefectures to immediately commence organization. The basic content of the proposal is roughly as follows:

"Outline of the Voluntary Police Officer System" (1) Each prefecture should, based on the following qualifications, begin investigation and registration: (A) Those with police officer experience and a robust physique eligible for pensions; (B) Those without pension eligibility but with police officer experience and personal desire; (C) Those without police officer experience but with firefighter experience and a desire among youth corps members. (2) Using the registration system, the first phase of organization will center around each police station, and the second phase will center around the prefecture, with group training provided. (3) In wartime or during incidents requiring a large number of police officers, outstanding individuals may be selected from the voluntary police officers and appointed as police officers. (4) Voluntary police officers will regularly receive training stipends, and substantial compensation will be provided in the event of casualties during incidents. (5) The authority of voluntary police officers will be defined accordingly. The establishment of the system will be funded with subsidies from the national treasury. (31st Hua Lian News Agency dispatch)

Matsuoka Arrives in Washington, Plans to Meet with Key US Government Figures, Makes Grandiose Statements to the Press 26

(Washington) Japanese delegate to the League of Nations, Yosuke Matsuoka, arrived here today and told people that he intends to stay for at least three days, visiting various key figures in the US government and seeking an audience with the President, though he has no specific mission, merely an informal discussion. (30th National Telegram)

(Washington) Japanese delegate to the League of Nations, Yosuke Matsuoka, declared to press representatives, "The United States and Japan are the two major powers of the Pacific and should maintain amity to safeguard peace. Japan is not China's enemy and desires to see China well-organized so that Japan can smoothly sell its merchandise." He also stated that Japan does not desire to rule China, and the fact that the United States abandoned the Philippines, as well as the difficulties faced by Britain in handling its territories, further dissuade Japan from the idea of ruling China. Matsuoka further said that the concentration of the entire US Navy fleet in the Pacific is actually a source of anxiety for Japan. Because Japanese public opinion is divided, the government has temporarily shelved negotiations for a non-aggression treaty with Russia, but it would be very beneficial for Japan and Russia to jointly organize a Manchurian committee to resolve the Siberian border dispute. The main point of divergence between the opinions of Japan and the United States lies in the matter of the permanent stationing of Japanese troops in Manchuria. Japan must protect "Manchukuo" and therefore it is necessary to station troops in Manchuria. The United States once adopted the Monroe Doctrine in South America, and Japan's situation in China is exactly the same. He also said that Japan would only invade inside the Great Wall if China took provocative action. As for the mandated territories in the Pacific islands after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, there would be absolutely no problem. In closing, Matsuoka denied the rumors circulating that Japan was building fortresses on the Pacific mandated islands, saying there was no such thing. (31st Havas dispatch)

Sino-Soviet Relations Worsen Over Chinese Eastern Railway Issue 27

Soviet Russia Detains Over 4,000 Railway Cars; Japan Instigates Puppet Manchukuo to Demand Three Items

(Tokyo) According to diplomatic sources, the Japanese Foreign Ministry is taking a provocative approach towards Russia over the Chinese Eastern Railway issue for two reasons: Firstly, the Japanese have been secretly planning to seize the Chinese Eastern Railway for several years, but the opportunity had not yet arrived. However, the strong demands of the puppet Manchukuo Foreign Ministry continues and now there is an opportunity to instigate an incident. Secondly, it is a diplomatic constraint policy. The Japanese Foreign Ministry believes that since Hitler came to power, he has vigorously pursued an anti-Russian policy, and British-Russian relations have deteriorated due to the arrest of British engineers. Japan is taking the opportunity to make things difficult for Russia, in order to achieve its long-cherished goals. (31st Lianhua Telegram)

(Harbin) Since the outbreak of the Manchurian Incident, Soviet Russia has advocated international transportation and transported 4,500 locomotives and freight cars from the Chinese Eastern Railway to its own country. Despite repeated negotiations by "Manchukuo," they have refused to return them. Recently, they even plan to transport all the locomotives and freight cars of the Chinese Eastern Railway. On the 29th, "Manchukuo" blocked the transportation of Chinese Eastern Railway trains into Soviet Russia from the eastern and western borders of Manchouli and Borazitayevo. Relations between Russia and Manchukuo, centered around this transportation issue, are gradually becoming precarious and warrant serious attention. (31st Dentsu dispatch)

(Tokyo) According to a dispatch from Changchun, "Manchukuo" now wishes to resolve the issue of Chinese Eastern Railway freight cars with Soviet Russia in a moderate manner. It is said that there are a total of 4,000 freight cars and several passenger cars that have entered the Siberian Railway. The "Manchukuo" authorities have now put forward the following requests: (1) The locomotives and cars of the Chinese Eastern Railway shall not be allowed to enter the Siberian Railway in the future; (2) Freight cars transporting grain must comply with the normal tax regulations; (3) The distribution of the income of the Chinese Eastern Railway must be revised so that Soviet Russia and "Manchukuo" are on an equal footing. It is said that the above are the minimum requirements. The "Manchukuo" authorities are now expressing a spirit of goodwill, but at the same time, they are also expressing their determination to have their demands respected. According to a dispatch from Changchun, on March 28, Russian personnel of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Manchouli attempted to drive four locomotives into the Siberian Railway but were stopped by local "Manchukuo" officials. (31st Reuters dispatch)

Japan and Siam Seek Amity; Siamese Minister of Railways Invited to Visit Japan 28

(Tokyo) Siam, which abstained from voting and sided with Japan when the League of Nations General Assembly decided on a resolution, is gradually becoming closer to Japan. Japanese Railway Minister Tadatsugu Mitome invited the Siamese Minister of Railways to visit Japan in order to increase the amity between the two countries. This plan was made early on the 31st. However, Siam proceeded rather quickly after abstaining at the General Assembly. As a result of the Railway Ministry's request to the Foreign Ministry for negotiations, it has obtained the consent of the Siamese authorities. The Japanese Railway Ministry has decided to treat him as a guest of the Railway Ministry and invite him to inspect the actual situation of Japanese railways and commerce and industry. At the same time, it will express its gratitude for his actions in Geneva. It is said that the Siamese Railway Minister will visit Japan in mid-April when the cherry blossoms are in full bloom. (31st Japan Federation News Agency dispatch)

Pirates Hijack Ships and Kidnap People Outside Newchwang

British Maritime Association Asks Foreign Ministry for Rescue

Japanese Aircraft Conduct Reconnaissance for Pirate Traces with No Results

Newchwang: The Newchwang coastal reconnaissance team is pursuing the pirates with the support of Japanese officials after British crew members were kidnapped, but no clues have been found. However, the pirates appear to have landed at Jiegou and fled towards Qingshui Gou. (31st Dentsu dispatch)

(London) The Merchant Navigation Association, organized by British certified captains and crew members, protested to the Foreign Office today over the kidnapping of four crew members of the Nanchang steamer and requested prompt rescue measures. The association, based in Liverpool, issued a statement today saying that the news of such atrocities has shocked the shipping industry. British ships have been repeatedly attacked recently, and all those kidnapped by pirates have been subjected to various forms of abuse. This case is particularly egregious. Among the four kidnapped crew members, one, a Mr. Johnson, has a mother who has lost her memory for two years due to grief over the loss of her daughter. Now that her son has suffered an accident again, people dare not tell her. (30th Reuters dispatch)

Newchwang: Several Japanese aircraft flew around Newchwang yesterday to scout for traces of the pirates who kidnapped four British people from the Nanchang steamer on Wednesday, but found nothing. A large-scale reconnaissance will be conducted today. (31st Reuters dispatch)

(Beiping) It is now known that the four crew members kidnapped from the Nanchang ship are all young men under the age of thirty, none of whom are married and none of whom speak Chinese. People here believe that the four kidnapped British people can be expected to be found soon, because there are no shelters on the ground in the four rural areas, unlike last year when Mrs. Pawley and others were kidnapped when sorghum was everywhere. According to the detailed information now available, the case occurred at 11:43 a.m., when two civilian ships, seemingly innocuous, approached the Nanchang ship. Soon eight people jumped onto the Nanchang ship, several of whom were wearing uniforms. After boarding the ship, they fired handguns indiscriminately, wounding two Chinese people on board. The four crew members in the kitchen were unable to draw their guns in time and were subdued by the pirates. Their aim was undoubtedly to kidnap foreigners. After hastily looting the crew members' cabins, the pirates took the four crew members away. When they went from the big ship to the civilian ship, there were another ten bandits in the small boat to provide support. (31st Reuters dispatch)

Center of European Politics Shifts to Paris; Little Entente Representatives Inquire About France's Intentions; Counterproposal to the Four-Power Pact Planned 65

Full Text of the Four-Power Pact Reported by French Newspapers 66

▲Reuters Paris, 31st: This morning, various newspapers here published the full text of the so-called agreement reached by British Prime Minister MacDonald and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini in Rome, containing the following six provisions: (1) Germany, France, Italy, and Britain undertake to develop an effective cooperation policy in order to maintain peace; (2) The four countries reaffirm the principle of revising the peace treaty, but this must be done within the structure of the League of Nations; (3) France, Britain, and Italy declare that if disarmament is only partial, then Germany's equal rights should have effective meaning. Germany undertakes to negotiate with other powers to gradually realize this equality. The same compromise should be made regarding Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria; (4) All political and non-political problems in Europe and beyond, including colonial areas, should be addressed as far as possible with a common approach; (5) The agreement is for a term of ten years; (6) The agreement should be registered with the League of Nations.

World Economic Conference May Move to Washington 67

England and France Seek Urgent Solution to War Debt Problem

The United States Shows a Tendency to Reduce Tariffs

▲ National, Washington, 30th - Reliable sources say that President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull have good reason to believe that France will soon pay the arrears of its December war debt. It is also reported that there is a movement to move the World Economic Conference from London to Washington, to be convened around May. These two pieces of news suggest that the U.S. government anticipates that the war debt issue can be resolved before the economic conference is convened. It is reported that the U.S. government is preparing to begin talks on war debt as soon as Congress resolves domestic emergency issues. The various records exchanged between Secretary of State Hull and British Ambassador Lindsay have been studied by experts, and it is said that the records collected this time are extremely detailed, with some parts to be used in the economic conference. Therefore, many parties believe that since these records have been sent to the U.S., and the economic experts from England and France will be sent to the U.S. to discuss war debt, it might as well move the economic conference to Washington. In addition, there is another piece of news that many foreign correspondents believe to be true: if the economic conference is convened here and the war debt is resolved by then, the United States will be willing to greatly reduce tariffs, as long as other countries can do the same. It may also make other contributions to promote international trade. Congressional leaders have stated that there is a majority in both houses in favor of reducing tariffs.

▲ National, Washington, 30th - The general sentiment in Washington tonight is that the Democratic government has found a way to revise the war debt foundation, which will satisfy both Congress and the debtors. It is anticipated that a war debt conference can be held within two weeks. Although this statement has not been confirmed by the White House, friends of the President and Secretary of State believe that informal talks between the State Department and the British and French ambassadors have produced some proposals that can lead to a formal conference. As for the revision of the war debt foundation, it is rumored that some important people are in favor of postponing the war debt due on June 15, and then adopting a plan with a total amount not exceeding twelve, funded by the issuance of public bonds.

British Government Attaches Importance to the Arrest of British Nationals 68

Recalls Ambassador to Moscow to Hear Report Before Determining Attitude, May Resort to Excluding Russian Goods

▲ Havas, London, 30th - Regarding the arrest of British Vickers Company engineers in Moscow, a question was raised in the House of Commons today, to which Foreign Secretary Simon replied that the government had recalled the British Ambassador to Russia, Sir Esmond Ovey, to return to the country, and will determine a solution after his report. Political circles interpret this attitude as the government's intention to delay the matter by waiting for the British ambassador to return and report before deciding on British-Russian relations. It is recalled that Simon recently declared that a firm attitude must be adopted towards Soviet Russia, but Prime Minister MacDonald believed that a moderate attitude should be adopted. Therefore, it is not yet known what attitude the government will take. However, it will take some time for the British Ambassador to Russia to return and report. It is possible that the Soviet Russia may change its attitude during this time. It is generally believed that the inside story of this incident is a scene set by the Soviet Russian government's police department. In fact, the Soviet Russian government already knows that the British engineers are innocent, and within a few days, it hopes to obtain a solution that will satisfy Britain. In this way, the measures demanded by British cabinet members and most of the public opinion, which are inconsistent with British interests, can also be avoided.

▲ National, Moscow, 30th - The Russian government issued a communiqué today, announcing that the trial of the British engineers of the Vickers Company is scheduled to open on April 9. The defendants will be charged with espionage and other charges. According to criminal law, the most severe punishment is execution by firing squad. It is reported that on the 12th of this month, the Soviet Russian authorities arrested several Russians and six British engineers. Later, two British men were released, and three British men were allowed bail. The remaining one person was detained and not released. The British government and the British ambassador repeatedly negotiated to no avail. At the time of the publication of this communiqué, British Ambassador Sir Esmond Ovey and his family were being recalled to the country and departing for England. The diplomatic corps all went to the station to see him off, but the Russian Foreign Affairs Committee did not send a representative to see him off. Although the British government stated that Sir Ovey will return to his post, it is said in official circles that Sir Ovey may not return after returning to the country. Considering the current situation, the attitudes of the British and Russian governments are equally firm, and it seems that there may not be any change.

▲ Reuters, London, 31st - Regarding the statement made by Latham in the Australian Parliament that Britain would exclude Russian goods from entering the country, it is now learned that the British government has not yet made this decision. It is unlikely that there will be such a move before the cabinet meeting on Monday next week.

Germany Vigorously Implements Anti-Jewish Movement Starting Today 70

Nazi Party Leads People to March and Demonstrate

Said to be Intended to Resist the Anti-German Tide Abroad

▲ Reuters, Berlin, 30th - The central party headquarters of the National Socialist Party in Munich issued an official announcement today, stating that the National Socialist Party will hold a nationwide anti-Jewish movement starting at 10 a.m. on Saturday (April 1), without delay. This morning, National Authority Party leader Hugenberg and Chancellor Hitler discussed the anti-Jewish movement. The Jewish people's panic about the anti-Jewish movement can be seen in the market. Today, the market price plummeted due to the sale of stocks worth millions of marks.

▲ National, Munich, 30th - The Anti-Jewish Committee issued a declaration tonight, ordering all places to implement a boycott of Jewish shops and various businesses starting on Saturday. Even Jews who have converted to Christianity are included in the boycott. Pickets will be placed in front of each store to prevent customers from entering, but they must not be physically harmed or take actions such as smashing windows, resulting in material losses. All Jewish businesses will be marked with huge black and yellow signs. Boycotted stores must not open non-Jewish employees, and parades will be held, carrying flags with slogans, to persuade the public to boycott Jewish stores. Such slogans will be posted in all cities and towns on Saturday morning.

▲ National, Berlin, 30th - The National Socialist Party's boycott of Jewish people is scheduled to begin at 10 a.m. on April 1. The General Committee of the National Socialist Party Boycott issued a declaration to the people of Munich today, inviting them to hold a public demonstration in Konigsplatz on Friday night. Bavarian Interior Minister Wagner will attend the meeting and give a speech.

▲ National, Berlin, 31st - National Socialist groups have petitioned the authorities, stating that Jewish people only account for one percent of the German population, so the Jewish school children admitted to each school in the future must not exceed one percent.

▲ National, Frankfurt, 31st - The chief justice has asked Jewish judges to resign voluntarily. Those who refuse to do so will not be allowed to enter the court again. The number of Jewish lawyers in the Frankfurt court will be determined by comparing the total population of Germans and Jewish people. The Jewish population is only slightly less than one percent of the German population.

The Tragedy of American Farmers (Continued) 76

New York Correspondence

"Debt"

In many places, the interest on farmers' debts is even higher than taxes. At present, American farmers have more than nine trillion gold dollars in real estate mortgage loans alone, and other various debts amount to about three trillion gold dollars. In this way, the debts of American farmers total as much as twelve trillion to thirteen trillion gold dollars. There are more than six million farm households in the United States, so each household has an average of two thousand gold dollars in debt. The annual interest on mortgage loans alone amounts to six hundred and seventy-one million gold dollars. One-tenth of the farm households owe as much as three-quarters of all their property, and one-fifth of the farm households owe half of their property. All of these are calculated based on the price on the land contract. In fact, as a result of farmer bankruptcies, land prices have fallen even further. According to the Hoover Commission report, in the past ten years, the price of farmland in the United States has fallen by a total of two trillion gold dollars. The property of countless farm households, when converted, is not enough to repay the debt. More than two-thirds of these debts are held by banks and insurance companies. Therefore, a question naturally arises: Who is the true owner of the farmland, the farm households who have no hope of repaying the debt, or the banks that control them? The property of thousands of farmers who are unable to repay their debts has been confiscated and auctioned by banks.

In the past decade or so, the rapid development of tenant farmers in the United States is also due to this. After farmers mortgage their own property, they become tenant farmers. Fifty years ago, when virgin land in the United States was about to be occupied, tenant farmers accounted for only a quarter of all farm households. Now it is almost half (42%). American farmers pay more than seven hundred million gold dollars in rent each year, which is even more than the interest on debt or taxes. With the current plummeting prices of agricultural products, the suffering of American tenant farmers is difficult to describe in words.

Now most farmers' income is not even half of the wages of hired farm workers in the past. In the first year of the economic panic, about one-third of the farm households sought side jobs to supplement their household income. Furthermore, most of the farmland freely abandoned by farmers is barren and becomes government land. This kind of government land, which was first seen in American history, is not only decreasing but also increasing day by day. In any case, the fact is that American farmers are gradually no longer the true owners of their own property. Capitalism in the era of panic either drives farmers off their land or turns them into lifelong debtors, unfree tenant farmers, who are even worse than hired farm workers.

"Tractors Have Become Weapons That Impoverish Farmers" One of the characteristics of capitalism is that the progress of technology and the application of new agricultural machinery have a great relationship in this mass bankruptcy of farmers. The use of tractors and combines in the United States has even more forcefully pushed farmers into the abyss. Machinery increases production, which in turn promotes the fall in prices. The past decade in the United States can be regarded as an era of great revolution in agricultural technology. The number of tractors used in agriculture reached 900,000. From 1922 to 1926 alone, this increased production by more than a quarter, while the planting area did not increase. The result was simply a sharp drop in prices and the bankruptcy of small farmers.

At the same time, the increase in productivity has created surplus laborers. In the vast plains of the United States, a worker can manage about 300 acres of planting area using new machinery. Since there is nowhere to accommodate the surplus population, the result is that the American countryside is piled up with a large number of idlers who have nothing to do, which only intensifies the competition in the labor market. In 1917, there were a total of 35,000 wheat-growing farm households in Montana. Now there are only 14,000 households. Where have the 21,000 farm households in that state who have been displaced by machinery gone? How do they live?

The application of tractors and combines in the United States has also had another result: tractors have bankrupted middle farmers and poor farmers, and promoted the rapid growth of rich farmers and large capitalist agriculture. Even the Hoover Commission had to say, "The number of middle farmers is decreasing day by day." According to the 1930 census statistics, between 1920 and 1930, only the number of middle farmer lands decreased. On the contrary, the number of poor small farm households (those with less than 19 acres) and large farm households (those with more than 500 acres) both increased greatly. For example, the land owned by farm households with 1,000 to 5,000 acres of land increased from 106 million to 127 million acres, an increase of 20%. The land owned by farm households with more than 5 acres of land increased from 113 million to 148 million acres, an increase of about one-third. Therefore, in countries with capitalist panic, the result of the use of tractors is like this: poor small farm households are increasingly divided, middle farm households go bankrupt, and rich farmers increase day by day. This situation is even more obvious in pure wheat-growing areas. For example, in the western states where tractors are most popular, the number of farm household lands with more than 1,000 acres has increased by more than half.

"Acreage Reduction Movement"

Naturally, in this tragic situation, farmers cannot but seek other ways to survive. Anti-tax and anti-debt movements, as well as preventing banks or government agencies from auctioning agricultural products, are often heard of. In some places, farmers openly gather crowds to kill judges, inspectors, and court officials who supervise auctions. In some places, thousands of farmers gather on their own to auction off land and agricultural implements at extremely low prices, not allowing others to participate. A cow or horse is sold for only a dime or five cents. The land or agricultural tools sold in this way can still be used by the original owner.

This primitive movement first occurred in the western states and is now spreading to many states and gradually entering the eastern states. In fact, many states have formed an "illegal" situation, and the law and its supervisors have lost their effectiveness. "In a sense," said the editor of the Evening Post, "this is a true peaceful revolution against the current order, the purpose of which is to eliminate heavy burdens." When the House of Representatives met on February 3, New York State Representative Galji said that not only a "peaceful" revolution was possible, but also compared the farmers' actions to the Boston Riot when the American Revolutionary War broke out.

Naturally, the American authorities have also tried to ease the situation. Some large banks and insurance companies have voluntarily announced a temporary suspension of auctions. Senator Hall proposed a two-year moratorium on national debt payments. Some advocated finding ways to raise agricultural product prices, and some even advocated using inflationary policies to save the situation. The most famous of these plans is the so-called acreage reduction bill passed by the House, which stipulates that the difference between the current market price and the pre-war price will be compensated to farmers by the state establishing a special tax. However, farmers must leave most of their cultivated land barren in order to reduce production and increase prices. This is a funny thing.

However, these American plans will either provoke resistance from the banking industry and trusts, or they are only temporary attempts to survive. The "acreage reduction" bill has already been buried. All of these plans, at best, can only give temporary and weak comfort to the extremely poor farmers. The terrible agricultural panic is a product of capitalist development and panic, and can only be eliminated with its demise. (The End)

Cold Pass Frontline Position Inspection Record 77

Cold Pass Once Lost, Recovered by Shang Zhen's Troops

Enemy Suffered Losses and Retreated Over Twenty Li Beyond the Pass

Shang Army's Frontline Defensive Works Extremely Solid

But Military Supplies and Various Food Provisions Severely Lacking

Tianjin Special Dispatch: Nowadays, any armed comrades who truly are willing to sacrifice and vow to resist Japan are easily embraced by the fervent support of the national populace. It's not necessary to mention the past Nineteenth Route Army. Recently, Song Zheyuan's troops and Guan Linzheng's division fought bloody battles against Japan at Xifengkou and Gubeikou, both receiving unanimous support from the national populace. However, Division Commander Guan was isolated and without assistance, suffering too many casualties, so Gubeikou remains in enemy hands to this day. Cold Pass was once lost, but was recovered by Shang Zhen's dispatch of Huang Guanghua's division, a truly great achievement. At that time, Zhang Xueliang had not yet resigned, and concealing the loss of territory, he secretly did not make it public, thus the achievement of Shang's troops in recovering Cold Pass was also buried. To this day, Shang's troops still resist the enemy twenty li outside of Cold Pass, and their calm and steady spirit is also worthy of our praise. The reporter went to the front lines of eastern Luan on the 27th to inspect, and it happened that Shao Yuanchong and Lu Dangping were also going to eastern Luan, so we traveled together. At 11:30 a.m. that morning, we departed from the East Station on the third express train. At 2:00 p.m., we arrived in Tangshan and changed to the seventh slow train to Kaiping, then went to the headquarters of the 囗th Army Corps to visit Commander Shang. According to Shang, the loss of Chengde had a great impact on military affairs. The troops outside the Great Wall retreated without a fight. The enemy's Nakamura Brigade and Miyama Detachment (belonging to the 10th Division of the Jilu Army), about two thousand men, traveled in over a hundred vehicles including tanks, armored cars, and heavy trucks, departing from Lingnan. With tanks leading the way, they charged wildly, as if entering an uninhabited land. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month, the Miyama Detachment occupied Cold Pass. Our army was ordered to counterattack on the 5th, immediately sending Division Commander Huang Guanghua to lead his troops, advancing through the night, recovering Cold Pass on the 6th, and taking advantage of the victory to pursue the enemy over thirty li beyond the pass, occupying the two positions of Xiaojiayingzi and Madaogou. Miyama then led his troops to attack Xifengkou and Gubeikou. Miyama boasted that he was invincible, but then led his troops to attack Cold Pass again. We immediately met them head-on with a fierce attack, and also used night raids. The enemy suffered heavy losses. As the terrain of Xiaojiayingzi is low-lying, our army had to abandon it. We defended Madaogou on the front. The enemy was in Xiaojiayingzi, eight li away. Our left flank defended the Shanshen Temple and Yingtaoyuanzi, and our right flank defended Gaoligou and Badaohe. If the enemy attacked our front, our left and right flanks would encircle the enemy. If the enemy attacked our left and right flanks, our front would attack. If the enemy attacked all three routes at once, a large force would be required, but the terrain of Xiaojiayingzi is concave, and a large force cannot be deployed. Therefore, in recent days, the enemy has not dared to launch a formal attack, only relying on artillery and aircraft to harass us daily. Enemy aircraft harass us four times a day, four aircraft each time, from after 7:00 a.m. to 4:00 or 5:00 p.m. The first time is a reconnaissance plane, which does not drop bombs. The second, third, and fourth times are bombers, each plane dropping over ten bombs, about fifty or sixty bombs in total. The large and small villages inside and outside of Cold Pass were bombed very badly. For the first day or two, the people did not understand the danger. Seeing enemy planes fly over, they came out of their homes to look up. The enemy planes mistakenly thought they were troops, and dropped bombs, causing many civilian casualties. Afterwards, they all fled. When the planes dropped bombs and the artillery bombarded, our army's telegraph lines were often blown up. Even if they were not blown up, it was impossible to talk due to the continuous bombing sounds. At this time, the frontline radio station also lost its normal function because the air was shaken by the loud noises, and could not transmit messages. On the 25th and 26th, there were strong winds and rain, and the military telegraph lines were blown down. It was repaired this evening (the 27th). At that time, Lu Dangping told Shang that the Beijing People's Self-Defense Guidance Committee had achieved great results in raising funds, having collected over one million yuan, but they did not know what the front lines needed. Shang replied that shoes, socks, broadswords, stretcher beds, cars, and gasoline were all extremely needed. Lu Kun promised to return to Beijing to report to the Self-Defense Guidance Committee to purchase them. Then, we studied the time to go to the front lines, deciding to depart that night, arrive before dawn, and return at sunrise, as it would be dangerous after that time. Kaiping has East-West and North-South main streets. Business is depressed. There are city towers but no city walls. The entire city has about three or four thousand households. Food prices are even higher than in Tianjin. The discipline of Shang's army is very good, and the people praise it. When asked about the discipline of the Northeast Army, they shook their heads and sighed slightly. At 8:00 p.m. that evening, the reporter followed Shang Zhen, Shao Yuanchong, and Lu Dangping onto a special train. At 10:00 p.m., we arrived in Luanzhou, and immediately changed to a car to depart. From Luanzhou to Qian'an is ninety li, from Qian'an to Jianchangying is forty li, and from Jianchangying to Cold Pass is eight li. This road for cars was hastily repaired by Shang Zhen sending troops temporarily. Because it was crushed by heavy transport vehicles, it was rough and uneven. The car traveled bumpily, fearing it would overturn. At 1:30 a.m. on the 28th, we arrived in Qian'an, passing through the city. At 2:30 a.m., we arrived near Jianchangying's 囗囗囗. Because Jianchangying was destroyed by enemy aircraft, it was no longer habitable. The so-called 囗囗囗 was only a few dilapidated earth houses, which were temporarily found by Division Commanders Huang Guanghua and Gao Hongwen as a reception station. Charcoal was burned indoors to ward off the cold. Shang Zhen, knowing that there was no food on the front lines, brought some snacks and cigarettes, distributing them to everyone. Shang asked if thin porridge had been prepared. Division Commander Huang hesitated and replied, "There is no rice or millet, so it was not prepared." This one sentence already showed the suffering of the soldiers on the front lines. Division Commander Huang called his attendants to bring a few plates of crackers. Looking closely, they were infested with worms, but the soldiers regarded them as treasures. Huang and Gao both expressed that all the soldiers were willing to sacrifice themselves for the country and vowed to kill the enemy. Huang told the reporter that the enemy had over twenty artillery pieces, dozens of mortars, and many light and heavy machine guns. The battle on the 24th was the most fierce. The enemy launched a joint land and air attack with all their strength. The Madaogou position was lost and regained twice. Finally, our special service battalion commander Zhang Kexun led his troops to Xiaojiayingzi, approaching the enemy's trenches. He first threw hand grenades, but unexpectedly, the grenades were old and damp, and most did not explode. Otherwise, Miyama would have been completely annihilated. But because the grenades did not explode, they used broadswords to slash. Our Battalion Commander Zhang and Company Commander Meng ZhanKui, and Platoon Leader Ma Dengying charged into the enemy's machine gun positions and died heroically at the same time. From this battle, the enemy's courage has been chilled, and they dare not attack again, only using aircraft and artillery to harass us every day. Our soldiers are used to it and no longer fear it. We have anti-aircraft machine guns and have damaged an enemy plane. The enemy is very afraid and stays above two or three thousand meters, not daring to fly low, so the damage is minimal. I observe the enemy planes with binoculars every day. They are all old-fashioned biplanes, and the piloting skills are not very refined, so they cannot fly at night. Yesterday morning (the 27th), for the first time, enemy planes were found to be single-wing Junkers planes, equipped with machine guns. Each bomb weighed about two hundred pounds and created a pit over ten feet deep when it hit the ground. Our troops all have shelters, so there are few casualties. All work is done at night. Yesterday, enemy planes dropped bombs in Tangzhangzi, and one of our engineers repairing the telegraph lines was injured. Then, I spoke with Commander Shang. Shang said that supplies are lacking on the front lines because transportation is inconvenient and replenishment is difficult. Horse feed is especially lacking. Qian'an County has six districts. Song Zheyuan's troops occupy three districts. Our army's battlefield occupies one district. This battlefield district is all mountains, with no grass on the mountains, mostly planted with walnuts and chestnuts. Our army's reserve troops occupy one district, leaving one district, which is not enough to maintain the people's food supply, so how can it supply military use? Now, each division only has twenty stretcher beds. If there is a fierce battle, it will not be enough. I hope the rear will replenish them. The central government stipulates that for each officer killed in action, they are allowed to buy a coffin worth fifteen yuan, and for each soldier, they are allowed to buy a coffin worth twelve yuan. I feel very uneasy about this, and have issued orders to my subordinates that each lieutenant officer killed in action is allowed to purchase a coffin worth thirty yuan, and each soldier is allowed to purchase a coffin worth fifteen yuan. Officers above the rank of colonel will have special preferential treatment. The funds required will be advanced by me personally to comfort the heroic souls. At 3:30, all the cars departed again. Division Commander Huang also sent dozens of guards to go five minutes ahead to provide security. The reporter arrived at Cold Pass at 4:00. Getting out of the car, we immediately walked out of the pass. The moon was dark, the wind was mournful, and there was no sound of chickens or dogs, fully displaying the solemn scene of the battlefield. The lights in the mountains were dim, which I was told was the soldiers' work to protect against the cold. Then, we strode urgently on the sand. Meditating that in the South, the peach blossoms were red, the willows were green, the flowers were fragrant, and the birds were singing, while here it was still in an icy world with a biting north wind. On the way, we met a stretcher team carrying a wounded soldier. Shang immediately stepped forward to express his condolences, learning that he was an engineer who had been wounded by enemy bombing in Tangzhangzi that morning. After traveling six or seven li, we inspected several defensive works. As the east was just beginning to brighten, the rumbling of enemy artillery reached our ears. Everyone did not want to go forward, but Shang remained calm, and led us up the mountain to view the bunkers and trenches, as well as the machine gun positions, which were all new fortifications after the European War. Because the mountain's steep slopes made the sand very slippery, two people lost their footing and fell. At this time, we had just reached the mountainside, and Shang still wanted to lead us to see the artillery positions on the top of the mountain, but everyone sighed at the mountain and returned in disappointment. At 6:00, we returned to Cold Pass. Someone suggested climbing to the top of Cold Pass to see the majestic appearance of the Great Wall, but because although the mountain was not high, it would take three hours to go up and down, and we were afraid that the enemy planes would arrive before we reached the top, so we gave up. Under the pass, there were still a few dilapidated houses. Among them, there were residents, who were opening the door to fetch water, without any panic or anxiety. This was strange indeed. In a mountain cave half a li outside the pass, there was a dead body, a soldier of the Northeast Army who had been killed by enemy fire during the retreat. Division Commander Huang immediately ordered it to be buried as soon as possible. Then, we met one or two hundred civilians, carrying hoes and spades, standing on the side of the road, all smiling bitterly. According to Division Commander Huang, the requisitioned civilians did not receive wages. Fortunately, the villagers still knew how to love their country, working at sunrise and resting at sunset, without any complaints. The reporter expressed his great admiration for the solid and meticulous defensive works, and believed that if Zhaoyang, Kailu, and other places had these works, Rehe would not have easily fallen into enemy hands. Shang laughed and said, "Having good works also requires good soldiers. Otherwise, if they run away as soon as they see the enemy, even if there are good works, they will be given to the enemy." At 6:30, we boarded the car and left Cold Pass. At 9:00, we arrived at 囗zhou and immediately boarded the special train. At 11:00, we arrived in Kaiping. Shang insisted on inviting us to get off the car for lunch. After lunch, he gathered over a hundred generals and officers and invited Shao to give a speech. At 3:30 p.m., Shang prepared a special car to send us to the station to say goodbye. At 7:00 p.m., we arrived in Tianjin, already exhausted. (March 29th)

Great Fire at Shenxin Cotton Mill in Hankou 78

Losses Estimated at Approximately Two Million Yuan, Over Four Thousand Workers Unemployed

Hankou Dispatch: The Shenxin Cotton Mill in Zongguan, Qiaokou, in this city, is the largest enterprise organization independently run by Chinese people, with a capital of approximately three million yuan, divided into three sections: spinning, weaving, and warehousing, employing over four thousand male and female workers. On the 29th, because all the workers participated in the memorial meeting for the seventy-two martyrs, they were given a day off, leaving only one foreman and four workers to take care of the factory. Unexpectedly, at 4:00 p.m., a fire suddenly broke out. Due to the small number of people, it was difficult to extinguish, and it became a major disaster. Buildings and machinery were reduced to ashes. Initially, the foreman Lu A'gen and workers Zhang Yougen, Zhang Jiyuan, Hu Xingjia, and Lu Qiuquan, a total of five people, were still organizing the earth axis in the fine yarn room after all the workers left the factory. At 4:00 p.m., they had not yet finished. At 4:30 p.m., a fire suddenly broke out under the earth axis, and the fire was very fierce. Lu and the others immediately went outside to call for help. Because the other workers had all been given a holiday, they could not be gathered in time, causing the fire to become more intense. Fire brigades from various places rushed to the scene, but were unable to extinguish the fire. It continued to burn until 1:00 a.m. this morning (30th), when it was finally extinguished. All the steel wire room, coarse yarn room, fine yarn room, reeling room, and carding room, over four hundred and eighty buildings, were all reduced to scorched earth. Only the opening room and the cloth factory were not burned. After investigation, the losses are estimated at over two million yuan, accounting for seven-tenths of the total capital. It will be difficult to resume work in a short period of time. The four thousand workers who rely on it for food and clothing have suddenly become unemployed. On the 30th, the workers elected representatives to contact the factory and the authorities, requesting relief. The city party headquarters and the municipal government have already discussed it once and decided to actively find ways to maintain it. The garrison command and the Public Security Bureau have sent police to temporarily station at the fire scene to maintain order. The factory manager, Li Guowei, also telegraphed the Shanghai factory to report the details of the negligence. It was found that the factory had previously insured for 1,298,900 taels of fire insurance, which expired on the 15th of this month, and then insured for another 1,000,000 taels, which had not yet been registered with the local police station, before the fire broke out. However, since the people boycotted inferior goods since last year, the factory's business has been quite prosperous. The true cause of the fire is still unknown. The nine people who discovered the fire, including Lu A'gen, were sent to the Public Security Bureau on the 30th to await interrogation.

In Zongguan, Qiaokou, in addition to the Shenxin Cotton Mill, there is also the Taian Cotton Mill run by the Japanese. Because cotton merchants do not sell raw materials and the cotton mill does not purchase products, it announced the suspension of work on the 28th. The garrison command, deeply concerned that the factory originally employed many Chinese workers and that labor-capital negotiations might occur between the unemployed workers and the factory, leading to disputes, ordered the First District Command, the Hankou Public Security Bureau, and the investigation department of the garrison command to pay close attention and strictly protect it. If there are unresolved problems between labor and capital, the workers should be advised to abide by the main points of the previously promulgated proclamation, request the competent authorities to negotiate or provide relief on their behalf, and absolutely not to directly negotiate. The workers should also be informed that they must not stay in the factory or make unreasonable disturbances, otherwise they will be arrested immediately. (March 30th)

Zhenjiang Suspected Enemy Goods Detained 80

The Zhenjiang National Salvation Association recently discovered several pieces of suspected enemy goods with flower labels transferred by Yuanda Cloth Store and immediately detained them. However, these cloths were all produced by Shanghai Lunchang Dyeing and Weaving Company. Afterwards, the merchant reported to the British Consul and requested that they be returned. The British Consul sent a letter to the Zhenjiang County Government for investigation. It is now reported that the Zhenjiang County Government has replied according to the letter from the Provincial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, stating that the raw materials of the goods are similar to enemy goods, and there is a fear that they may be mixed with counterfeit goods in an attempt to profit. After consultation, it was decided to report to the province to consult the Ministry to send personnel to thoroughly investigate whether the products of the company are goods with changed labels. Before proof is obtained, they will be temporarily withheld.

Li Liejun Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 82

Li Discusses in Detail the Trip to Shanxi and Chahar to Meet Yan and Feng

Issues a Written Statement Describing the Opening of Political Power

Guowen News Agency reports that Central Committee Member Li Liejun previously left Shanghai to go north to inspect the war situation, and on behalf of Chairman Chiang, went to Shanxi and Chahar to meet with Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang to discuss major military plans for resisting Japan. He returned south from Ping on the previous day, advocating the opening of political power during the national crisis. At 5:50 p.m. yesterday, Li returned to Shanghai from Nanjing on the Nanjing-Shanghai train, accompanied by his private secretary Zhang Migong. In addition to issuing a face-to-face statement on the opening of political power, Li also spoke in detail with reporters about his trip to meet Yan and Feng.

(Process of Meeting Feng and Yan) After being summoned to Nanjing, I (Li Liejun refers to himself below) immediately studied with the Central Committee comrades the strategies to save the country from danger. The comrades were all able to discuss with sincerity, which is a good phenomenon. Later, as Rehe was in danger, I was extremely concerned and still decided to go north. Unfortunately, on the way, I heard the news of the fall of Chengde, and my heart was burned. I felt even more anxious, ashamed that I had no single soldier available to fight against the violent Japanese on the front lines. I met with Mr. Yan Baichuan several times in Taiyuan. Mr. Yan's attitude towards resisting Japan was extremely resolute, and he said that the one hundred thousand brave soldiers of Shanxi must stand on the front line of resisting Japan. His troops had all been mobilized and sent to the Chahar border. Some people often say that the Shanxi army is weak, but this is not the case. For example, the troops of Shang Zhen, who recently repeatedly defeated the violent Japanese at Lengkou, are indeed from the Shanxi army. Other troops, such as those of Fu Zuoyi, Li Fuying, and Yang Aiyuan, are all very reliable. If the Japanese army invades the west, they will definitely be given a major blow. Later, I took a car from Taiyuan to Zhangjiakou to meet the commoner Feng Huanzhang. Mr. Feng's opinion was as it was in the past. Regarding the resistance against Japan, Mr. Feng's position is active and tough, and he absolutely does not advocate holding on to a fixed position. As for the news repeatedly reported in the newspapers that he had a message for Nanjing, Mr. Feng repeatedly stated that resistance against Japan must be on the front lines, and one must truly fight and kill the enemy. It is said that he does not want to hide in the rear to avoid disaster. The Central Committee is still considering the 　Chen of Feng. Now the Japanese army also intends to invade Zhangjiakou, and Mr. Feng will soon be in the line of fire.

(Suggestion to Open Political Power) Given that the national crisis is becoming increasingly urgent, if the people of the whole country do not unite, the country will certainly perish. Therefore, I suggested opening political power, and I repeatedly talked about this with Chairman Chiang in Baoding. Mr. Chiang also deeply realized the mistakes of the past, so after I arrived in Nanjing, I formally submitted it to the Central Political Council. Mr. Wang and the comrades all agreed with this proposal, and it was decided to convene a National People's Congress on July 1 to truly entrust the central government to the people. At the same time, talent from all over the country will be gathered to manage the central government. If there is internal unity, it will be easier to resist foreign insults.

(Regarding the Opening of Political Power) Regarding the opening of political power, Li issued a written statement stating that this time the Central Committee has determined the steps for opening political power in order to realize the Three Principles of the People. Although it is due to the demands of the times, very few members of the Kuomintang actually advocate dictatorship. This can be clearly understood by observing the course of the meeting and the statements made by Mr. Wang. However, in order to express the spirit, value, and sincerity of the resolutions to the world, the future conduct should be even more thorough. As Mr. Chiang said, it must be thoroughly opened. Upon returning to Shanghai, I plan to introduce the actual situation of the Central Committee's resistance against Japan and the sincerity of political reforms to society, hoping that the people of the country will know the truth and rise up in time.

Yang Dezhao Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 83

Yang Dezhao, representing Chen Jitang, accompanied by his wife, and Li Haoju and his wife, the secretaries of Wang Jingwei, arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong on the President Hoover yesterday morning at 8:00. A reporter from New Voice Agency met with him on the ship. Yang said that after meeting Chairman Chiang in Shanghai, he would go to Nanjing. The Guangdong anti-Japanese army will depart north as soon as they have met the Fujian troops. The following is a record of Yang's remarks:

Awaiting Chiang's Meeting: Yang said that I originally intended to take the Canadian Empress ship to Shanghai, but later changed to the President Hoover due to circumstances. After arriving in Shanghai, I plan to first visit Vice President Song to inquire about the exact date of Chairman Chiang's arrival in Shanghai. After awaiting Chiang's visit in Shanghai and reporting everything, I will go to Nanjing to visit President Wang.

Suppressing Bandits Militarily: After Chairman Chiang went north to resist Japan, the military affairs of suppressing bandits in Jiangxi have not stopped and are still actively progressing. Chairman Chiang's intention was to ask Mr. Chen Bonan to take on the task, but Mr. Chen could not take full responsibility due to the heavy burden of affairs in Guangdong. Yu Hanmou is only undertaking a part of the work. The title has not been decided and will only be known after meeting Chiang and Wang.

About to Set Out: The Guangdong side will send ○○ regiment to undertake the work of suppressing the Communists. Guangdong could have set out earlier, but the organization of the logistics team was lacking, and transportation required recruiting laborers. Because it was the spring plowing season, it was not easy to recruit them, so we had to recruit them from Hunan and Guangxi provinces. As soon as it is completed, they can be mobilized and set out within one or two days. In the future, approximately three-tenths of the resident troops will be dispatched first, and then gradually up to eight-tenths. As for Cai Tingkai, the commander of the Nineteenth Army, he has also decided to send troops to assist Rehe.

Financial Difficulties: The expenses for suppressing the bandits are relatively difficult. Previously, Guangdong's expenses were mostly obtained from donations from overseas Chinese, but recently, due to the failure of overseas Chinese businesses, the income has decreased by more than one million yuan each year. Export trade is also poor, resulting in a strange financial situation. Therefore, Guangdong's military expenses are only 50%. If the expenses for suppressing the bandits are truly not available this time, we can only ask the Central Committee for assistance, but this is not a blackmailing act, but out of necessity.

Assisting Rehe and Resisting Japan: As for Guangdong's dispatch of troops to assist Rehe and resist Japan, it is about to be mobilized. There are no provisions for any titles such as the National Salvation Army. The original independent Fourth Division number will still be used. After meeting with the Nineteenth Route Army troops from Fujian and arriving at a suitable location, they can set out.

Consistent Diplomacy: As for the Southwest's foreign policy position, it is naturally consistent with the Central Committee's, namely, resisting Japan and suppressing the Communists. Without resisting Japan, there is no diplomacy to speak of. It is only possible to conduct diplomacy after being able to resist Japan. This is the same as what Mr. Wang Jingwei said. As for myself, I did not meet Mr. Hu Zhantang in Hong Kong, so Mr. Hu did not give me a letter to bring. Only Mr. Chen Bonan had a letter to convey to Chairman Chiang, but this is a common occurrence. The content is nothing more than the above, hoping to resist Japan and suppress bandits. After the bandits are suppressed, we can resist Japan. There is a connection between suppressing the Communists and resisting Japan. As for a compromise diplomacy, it is certainly not something we dare to support. Not only does Mr. Chen personally hold this view, but generally all armed comrades also share the same view.

Cotton Yarn, Cloth, Miscellaneous Grains, and Oil Cake Transactions Change to Silver Dollar Standard 84

All Starting from This Month

Since the implementation of the silver dollar standard in this city, all businesses calculate their transactions in silver dollars. In the exchanges, the Gold Exchange's margin trading has been using the silver dollar standard since the 16th. The Chinese Securities Exchange and the Securities and Commodities Exchange have been using the silver dollar standard. The Cotton Yarn and Cloth Exchange and the Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Exchange will also switch to the silver dollar standard starting in April. The announcements are recorded below: (1) The Shanghai market is following the Ministry's order. Cotton yarn trading from the September period and cotton trading until the October period will all be priced in silver dollars. Cotton will be priced in units of five cents in silver dollars, and cotton yarn will be priced in units of one dime in silver dollars. In addition to notifying the Broker's Association, this is hereby announced. Chinese Cotton Yarn Exchange. (2) The Shanghai Exchange Supervisor's Public Letter No. 28 stated in brief, "According to the order of the Ministry of Finance, in preparation for the abolition of the tael, it is stipulated that the Shanghai market will generally use silver taels and silver standard currency, or old one-yuan silver coins with the original weight or fineness, with seven mace, one fen, and five li of regulation silver equal to one silver dollar, becoming a fixed exchange rate in order to achieve uniformity." It was ordered to comply. After submitting it to a temporary meeting of the Board of Directors, it was resolved that the Exchange Federation will still calculate the six-month period, which has already been sold, in silver taels. Starting from the nine-month futures, which will be auctioned on April 1, all will be calculated in silver dollars. The resolution has been recorded. The exchange should also handle it in the same way. The pricing of soybean cakes is still set at two and a half li. In addition to informing the Broker's Association and replying with a report, it should be recorded and announced. It is hoped that all brokers will be informed as necessary. This is hereby announced. In addition, the trading market will be closed for three days on the 1st, 3rd, 4th, and 5th as usual. Business will resume as usual on the 6th. This has already been announced yesterday.

Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company Donates 100,000 Yuan for National Salvation Through Aviation 85

丨丨For the purpose of training pilot talent丨丨

Recently, the call for national salvation through aviation has been extremely high. People in Shanghai have elected Mayor Wu Tiecheng as the general leader of the solicitation team and have re-appointed well-known figures from all walks of life and those enthusiastic about national salvation as team leaders. Jian Yuqie, the general manager of Nanyang Company, is one of the solicitation team leaders. Recently, it has been heard that he plans to donate 100,000 yuan in the company's name for the purpose of training aircraft pilots. It is noted that the company has donated a large amount of money to social charities over the years. This time, it has donated another 100,000 yuan for national salvation through aviation, which is truly commendable for its righteousness and courage. The letter to Mayor Wu is attached below.

"Respected Director Wu Tiecheng,

I received your letter of the 12th of this month, entrusting Yuqie as the leader of the Shanghai Solicitation Team of the Chinese Aviation Association. I am aware of my limited abilities and fear that I will not be able to fulfill the task. However, my patriotic heart dares not lag behind others. Moreover, I am deeply moved by your sincere trust and encouragement. I will strive to make achievements. I intend to donate 100,000 yuan in the name of our company for the purpose of training aviation talent. This has been telegraphed to the board of directors in Hong Kong for approval. As for the company's staff and workers, they are still free to make their own donations at any time. I believe that purchasing aviation fighter planes to meet the national crisis is the most urgent plan at present. However, training this kind of pilot talent is also a top priority. The United Kingdom currently has 1,062 aviation fighter planes and 10,352 incumbent officers and soldiers proficient in piloting. France has 1,730 aviation fighter planes and 36,800 incumbent officers and soldiers proficient in piloting. Italy has 1,507 aviation fighter planes and 22,193 incumbent officers and soldiers proficient in piloting. Japan has 838 aviation fighter planes and 3,500 incumbent officers and soldiers proficient in piloting. Other countries are too numerous to mention. In general, the strength of air combat power depends on both the number of aircraft and the number of personnel. In addition to manufacturing aviation fighter planes, they pay special attention to training pilot talent. All kinds of equipment are made as precise as possible, even at great expense. Therefore, they can produce a steady stream of talent to defend the country. Looking back at our country, the equipment for this kind of training is not common, so this kind of talent cannot emerge continuously. In this time of national crisis, I believe that we should raise funds to purchase aircraft and also pay attention to training pilot talent in order to be of help. I hereby submit a report on the progress of the solicitation, hoping that you will review it. Please stipulate the method of distribution for the 100,000 yuan donated by our company, and inform us of how to train this kind of pilot talent at any time. Our company will save the money and wait. I respectfully reply and wish you good health.

Sincerely, Jian Yuqie, March 29, 1933"

Unification of Traffic Management on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railways 86

Based on the principle of benefiting merchants and increasing transportation, the Ministry of Railways ordered the railway bureau to draft a plan for submission.

The Ministry of Railways originally planned to convert all passenger and freight cars on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways into through trains to facilitate travel. The principle has been decided. Yesterday, the management bureaus of the two railways were ordered to quickly draft a unified traffic management method for the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways in order to set a date for implementation. The original order from the Xinsheng News Agency's Beijing correspondent is excerpted below:

"It is found that although the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways nominally belong to the same bureau, the traffic management of the two railways is still independent. Passenger and freight trains have not eliminated regional barriers and are not connected to each other. The distribution of locomotives has not been planned as a whole to adjust surpluses and deficits. Outwardly, passengers and merchants feel inconvenienced. Inwardly, transportation efficiency will inevitably be sharply reduced. The intangible losses in personnel expenses and work efficiency are even greater. This is not the way to railway economics and loses the purpose of merging the two railways. The two railways are required to divide the accounting system due to foreign debt relations. However, the accounting separation is to calculate the profits and losses of each business, while the traffic unification is to seek the economic benefits of transportation for each other, which can be carried out simultaneously without contradiction. Now, the capital's ferry is about to open to traffic, and the responsible goods of each road have also implemented joint transportation. In order to increase the transportation of the two roads and develop the business of the two roads, it is necessary to quickly seek to unify the traffic management of the two roads. For this reason, the bureau is ordered to quickly draft a unified traffic management method for the two roads based on the principle of facilitating passengers and merchants on the two roads and increasing transportation efficiency internally, and submit it for verification."

According to the Xinsheng News Agency's Beijing correspondent, the Ministry of Railways expects that the through traffic of all passenger and freight cars on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways will be fully implemented by June 1 at the latest in order to connect the Jinpu Ferry after the Yangtze River is installed.
