Liao Chengzhi and Others Transferred to Shanghai Public Security Bureau 88

Lawyers showed their eloquence in court. The defendants' opposition to the transfer was invalid.

Liao Chengzhi, the son of Central Committee member He Xiangning, has recently been identified by the Shanghai Public Security Bureau as having communist suspicions. Director Wen Hongen specially sent Inspector Lu Keqin to the Old Zha Gate Patrol Room of the Public Concession on the afternoon of March 28 to request assistance in the arrest. The chief dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to house number 9, Wufu Lane, Shanxi Road, to arrest Liao Chengzhi and two other Min people, Luo Dengxian, and Yu Wenhua from Henan, who were also suspected of being communists. The next morning, they were transferred to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court for interrogation. They were all ordered to be detained pending further interrogation. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the continued trial. Because of her concern for her son, He Xiangning's old illness relapsed and she was bedridden at her residence and unable to attend court. However, many of her relatives and friends went to the first court of the Second Branch of the High Court to listen to the trial after 2 pm. In addition, the ladies and gentlemen who came to court to listen were as numerous as clouds, causing the spacious courtroom to suddenly

experienced overcrowding. Those who arrived later had no place to stand. The lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Ma Chang, who were appointed by He Xiangning to defend her son, and Cai Xiaobai, the defense lawyer for Luo and Yu, also appeared in court on time. At 2:30, Criminal Court President Yu Ye, Judges Zhao Zhengdong and Zhou Han, Prosecutor Zhang Junqing, and the clerk took their seats. First, several other appeal cases were announced. At 2:50, Liao Chengzhi, Luo Dengxian, and Yu Wenhua were summoned to begin the trial. The bailiffs brought Yu Wenhua, who was in the waiting room, along with Liao Chengzhi and Luo Dengxian, who were sitting in the corner of the court, into the defendant's box. The judge first ordered Gan Jingxian, the lawyer of the patrol room, to report on the progress of the investigation during the adjournment. According to lawyer Gan, the address of the third defendant, Liao Chengzhi, has not yet been verified. When questioning the first defendant, Luo Dengxian, he confessed that he met Liao Chengzhi through Yu Wenhua's introduction. According to the second landlord of No. 9 Wufu Lane, the house was rented by Yu Wenhua from him. In addition, no other evidence was found. Lawyer Wu Kaisheng immediately stood up and stated that regarding Liao Chengzhi's

Address problem, this lawyer urgently needs to declare that He, Liao's mother, originally planned to come to court in person to prove it, but He's old illness relapsed due to her worry about her son, and she cannot come today. However, she has written a letter to prove that her son actually lives with her. After Liao Chengzhi was arrested, detectives from the Old Zha Gate Patrol Room went to He's residence to inquire with detectives from the French Patrol Room. He told the detectives that her son lived in the house, and the detectives continued to ask which room he lived in. He saw that there were many people and was temporarily nervous, so he answered that he did not know, resulting in this misunderstanding and the problem of an unknown address. Fortunately, in the past three days, other than this point, the patrol room lawyer has stated that no other evidence has been found. The presiding judge immediately announced that this case was requested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau for assistance, and the representative of the Public Security Bureau should be asked to state his case. Zhan Jifeng, the legal advisor of the Public Security Bureau, then said that the evidence and agreement of the defendants in this case were very consistent, and the court should approve it. As for Liao Chengzhi, because Mr. Liao is the son of the martyr Liao Zhongkai, in theory, he should not have reactionary behavior, so please the court make a ruling according to the evidence and in accordance with the law. Subsequently, the defense lawyers for Luo and Yu argued that the Public Security Bureau is not a formal court,

According to the agreement, Article 6 and Article 13 of the Criminal Procedure Law cannot be transferred. Moreover, the facts of the crime (Center) Liao Chengzhi (Left) Luo Dengxian (Right) Yu Wenhua (National News Agency Photo)

have not yet been verified, so they expressed their opposition to the transfer. Wu Kaisheng also stood up to defend Liao Chengzhi, generally saying that your court and the mainland are both official agencies of the Republic of China, and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, President Yu Youren, Vice President Song Ziwen, and other government authorities have all sent telegrams to rescue him. It seems that it is more beneficial for Mr. Liao to be transferred to the mainland, but your court is a formal court and has the right to accept the case and does not need to transfer jurisdiction. However, Mr. Liao is the son of the martyr Zhongkai and his only son. Since his arrest, his mother, He, has been thinking about him abnormally, causing her old illness to recur. She fainted once yesterday and is still lying in bed weeping. For the meritorious adults of the party and the country, and their descendants,

are suffering this implication, how can they not be heartbroken? If there is a crime, it should be accurately proven according to the agreement before the transfer is allowed. Now that three days have passed and no evidence has been found, although there are three doubts, (1) the address problem has been proven by He's letter, (2) someone pointed out that he is a communist, this kind of verbal statement is without evidence and is not enough to be adopted and believed, (3) the notes found on his body are nothing more than IOUs and receipts for lending money to people, so these three points can also be self-defeating. At the end, lawyer Wu cited the example of Soviet personnel coming to China, saying that the Soviet Union is a communist dictatorship, and now we have good relations with it. All the people of the Soviet Union are communists. If these people come to China, can our country also convict them? In short, all countries have communists, and they cannot be convicted just because they are communists. Only those communists who have acts of plotting to subvert the government can be brought to justice. Subsequently, Inspector Lu of the Public Security Bureau reported on the

Case detection situation, saying that the communist Wang Qiliang was first captured on Gonghe Road in Zhabei. Wang confessed that he was the secretary of the National Federation of Trade Unions and expressed his repentance and surrender, willing to report the party's secrets. It was said that the communists were holding a meeting at No. 9 Wufu Lane that day, and the three defendants in this case would all attend. Luo Dengxian was the secretary of the party group of the General Federation of Trade Unions, Yu Wenhua was the uncle of Zhang Guotao, the commander of the Red Army, and Liao Chengzhi was the secretary of the National Seamen's Union. Because he filed a request to the patrol room to send detectives to the place, Liao and others were arrested. Many notes were found on Liao's body, one of which was written with the abbreviation of the Shanghai Anti-Imperialist League. Since there is this kind of evidence, the transfer should be approved in accordance with the established precedent for handling transfer cases. Lu still wanted to state the reasons, but the lawyers of the defendants all said that the legal points were stated by the representative lawyer of the Public Security Bureau, and asked the court to prohibit Lu from speaking, causing

a slight misunderstanding with Lu. Lu's attitude also turned fierce. Subsequently, Zhang Hanqing, a communist who surrendered himself, came to court to testify that he was a member of the Central Political Bureau of the Communist Party and had worked with the defendants. Luo Dengxian was also a member of the bureau and was later sent as a representative to Manchuria. Recently, he was the secretary of the party group of the General Federation of Trade Unions. Liao Chengzhi returned to China in May last year and served as the secretary of the party group of the Seamen's Union. In November last year, a meeting was held in Zhabei to discuss many measures to harm the Republic of China. Yu Wenhua was Zhang Guotao's uncle and had been convicted and imprisoned, etc. When questioned by the defendants, Luo Dengxian did not admit what Inspector Lu and Zhang Hanqing said. He said that he went to Manchuria as a volunteer army and had worked in a Japanese yarn factory. He had little education and did not know what reaction was. Yu Wenhua confessed that he was released from prison in July last year. Mr. Zhang happened to say that he met me in March last year, which is incomprehensible. The court asked what crime he was imprisoned for. He replied that it was also due to political suspicion. Finally, Liao

Chengzhi's confession, in addition to resolutely denying knowing Zhang Hanqing, also said that he did not expect to be treated favorably because of the glory of his father and mother, but what these people (referring to Lu Zhang) said could not be admitted and demanded unconditional release. The presiding judge then asked the patrol room lawyer if he had any comments on the transfer. Lawyer Gan then said that this case is an assistance case. Under normal circumstances, the Public Security Bureau has two people to prove it, and the transfer should not be opposed. However, if your court thinks that it wants to accept the case, the patrol room can also conduct an investigation, but the law is equal in nature, so it is not convenient to make a difference based on the status. Please consider it in court. After Yu's interrogation, Zhang Prosecutor had no opinion to express, so he and the two judges Zhao Zhou retired to discuss for a moment, and then re-ascended to announce the ruling that Luo Dengxian, Yu Wenhua, and Liao Chengzhi were transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the exhibits were also transferred together. The lawyers of Luo and Yu immediately filed an appeal orally and requested a stay of execution of the ruling, but they were finally rejected by the court. Therefore, Liao and the other three were taken to the Municipal Public Security Bureau by Inspector Lu.

Shanghai Municipal Council Solves Water Fee Problem 89

Organizing an Advisory Board

Recently, the Municipal Council is considering the issue of calculating the water bill for household use by meter, and how to properly arrange relief for poor users. Members of the bureau and representatives of the water company are negotiating, and Feng Bingyuan is participating in the discussion from an independent perspective. He has made many contributions to the proposed measures. The water meter system has only recently been widely implemented, and there is little experience in its use. If a permanent water price list is formulated at this time, it seems inappropriate. Therefore, Feng's suggestion is adopted to set a trial period first. During this period, it is hoped that sufficient materials and experience can be obtained to formulate a water meter charging system that can provide reasonable relief to poorer users and make the responsibilities of users at all levels fair. Now, the amount of water required by users at all levels has been estimated. During the trial period, an unequal minimum water price will be charged according to this amount. In places with higher rents, this water bill is slightly higher than the current water meter system. The rate gradually decreases as the rent decreases. In places with extremely low rents, the fee charged for the estimated amount of water is much lower than the current price. For water used beyond the estimated amount, it is calculated according to the lowest water rate. After the above measures are implemented, residents at all levels will have a certain amount of household necessities. The water price is the same as before the implementation of the water meter system for those with lower rents, and lower than the previous proportion of rent for those with higher rents. Now, a few examples are given for clarity, and the situation of water bills during the trial period is as follows:

Example 1: For those with rent between 125 taels and 150 taels, the monthly fixed amount is 11,000 gallons, and the minimum fee is 8 yuan and 25 cents. For excess, the fee is 7 jiao and 5 cents per thousand gallons.

Example 2: For those with rent between 70

Page 13

Taels and 80 taels, the monthly fixed amount is 9,500 gallons, and the minimum fee is 5 yuan and 63 cents. For excess, the fee is 5 jiao and 9 cents per thousand gallons.

Example 3: For those with rent between 45 taels and 50 taels, the monthly fixed amount is 7,700 gallons, and the minimum fee is 3 yuan and 56 cents. For excess, the fee is 4 jiao and 6 cents per thousand gallons.

Example 4: For those with rent below 10 yuan, the monthly fixed amount is 3,500 gallons, and the minimum fee is 6 jiao. For excess, the fee is 1 jiao, 7 fen and 8 li per thousand gallons.

During the trial period, it is also planned to organize an advisory board to solve all difficult problems. This advisory board is currently being organized.

Representatives of All Trade Unions in the City Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 90

Requesting Compulsory Enforcement of the Sanyou Dispute

Please Strictly Investigate the Zhengtai and Other Tragic Cases

The various trade unions in this city believe that the dispute over the shutdown of the Sanyou Industrial Society General Factory in Hudong has not been resolved for more than a year, and the workers are suffering unbearably. The tragic cases of the Zhengtai and Yonghe factories were hastily concluded, and the bereaved families are crying and begging for help. It was decided at a discussion meeting held at the General Federation of Trade Unions the other day to send Zhu Xuefan and other seven people as representatives to petition the municipal government yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

Petition to the Municipal Government

At 10:00 a.m. yesterday, the representatives Zhu Xuefan, Ye Xiangnie, Shao Xubai, Long Peiyun, Li Yongxiang, Zhou Xuexiang, etc., carrying a joint petition from the various trade unions, went to the Municipal Government at Fenglin Bridge to pay respects to Mayor Wu. When the mayor was out on official business, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun received them. First, the representatives stated that (1) the dispute over the Sanyou Factory case has lasted for more than a year because the capitalists have always resisted government orders and refused to accept the judgment, which has been delayed until now and has not been resolved. The lives of the workers are in a desperate situation. The municipal government should quickly enforce the arbitration by effective means. (2) The Zhengtai and Yonghe factories caused unprecedented tragedies due to mismanagement and boiler explosions. They were hastily concluded. Please strictly investigate and order the Social Bureau to reject the factory's record to value human life.

Mr. Yu's reply

Then Mr. Yu replied that (1) the Sanyou Factory case has been telegraphed by the Executive Yuan to be handled in accordance with the newly promulgated Labor Dispute Handling Law. The labor side has been ordered to directly request the court for enforcement, so the case can be resolved soon. Before the court executes it, the municipal government will send another letter to urge the execution. (2) Although the factory has reported that the aftermath of the two factory tragedies has been completed, the municipal government is still investigating the responsibility for the accident. If it is due to the factory's negligence, it will not be easily dismissed and will be thoroughly investigated. The representatives were satisfied and left.

City Government Approves Cooperative Experiment Zone Plan 96

Gradual Stage Yields Real Results

The city's Cooperative Affairs Committee, recognizing that promoting cooperative enterprises without establishing cooperative experiment zones is difficult to achieve effective results, drafted a plan, selected locations, and proceeded gradually. The aim was to stimulate citizens' interest in and understanding of cooperative enterprises. This plan has been submitted by the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs to the Municipal Government for approval and record. The Shanghai Cooperative Experiment Zone plan is excerpted below: To promote cooperative enterprises in the city, it is proposed to first select suitable locations and pilot cooperative experiment zones to arouse citizens' interest in and understanding of cooperation, thereby promoting the development of cooperative enterprises in the city. (Locations) There are three public housing estates in the city. The first public housing estate is located on Quan Jia An Road in Zhabei, the second public housing estate is located on Luban Road and Xietu Road, and the third public housing estate is located on Jiaotong Road in Zhabei. Among the three estates, the second estate has the most residents and a better environment. Therefore, it is designated as the pilot cooperative experiment zone for the city. After the second estate has achieved results, efforts will be made to organize cooperative enterprises in the first and third estates. (Methods) The methods are planned in two steps. The first step is to reorganize the existing consumer cooperative in the second estate to focus on both consumer and credit services. The second step is to organize cooperative enterprises such as production and utilization. The methods are described below: 1. Reorganize the existing consumer cooperative. The second public housing estate established a consumer cooperative in July of the 20th year. However, because the residents of the estate are mostly from the working class, most do not understand the meaning of cooperative societies and lack considerable interest. Therefore, the number of members is small. Moreover, due to the lack of capital and inflexible operation, the society's affairs have not developed much to this day. It is now proposed to reorganize the society into the Shanghai Cooperative Experiment Zone Second Public Housing Estate Cooperative. The steps to be taken are as follows: (1) After the reorganization of the society, its business will include consumption, credit, production, utilization, etc., and will be organized separately. However, the first step is to start with consumption and credit. (2) The general manager of the public housing estate and the administrators of the estate will be responsible for publicizing the meaning of the cooperative to the residents and encouraging them to join the cooperative. (3) The share capital of the consumer cooperative in the estate was originally set at five yuan per share, which is too high. The share price should be reduced to one yuan per share. It is best if members can pay the shares in full at once. If they cannot pay in full at once, they can pay in two or three installments, or deduct it directly from the members' purchase surplus. (4) The capital of the society should be collected from shares as much as possible. If the collected shares are not enough, a low-interest loan may be requested from the Bureau of Social Affairs, which shall be repaid in installments within one year from the society's surplus. (5) The estate has a poverty alleviation fund, which can be borrowed in the name of the estate's cooperative society and used as credit cooperative loans. (6) The society's procurement should focus on the daily necessities of the members, such as rice, firewood, and flour. The amount of procurement and the quality of the goods, as well as the internal expenses of the society, should be reduced as much as possible. Members should be encouraged to volunteer to serve in the society. (7) There are currently 937 male and female residents of the estate with productive capacity. The average monthly income of 213 people is from three to ten yuan, 716 people are from eleven to twenty yuan, and 8 people are from twenty-four to twenty yuan. It can be seen that most of the residents of the estate are in a state of poverty. If poverty is to be alleviated, credit cooperation must be carried out at the same time. The organization should be meticulous, and special attention should be paid to accounting to make it independent. The credit and morality of the members should be improved. On the one hand, the Bureau of Social Affairs should promote and reward it to promote the development of the society. 2. Organize cooperative enterprises for production and utilization, etc. Among the residents of the estate, 393 are rickshaw pullers, 29 are small cart pullers, 43 are grass shoe makers, 13 are reed curtain weavers, 11 are toothbrush threaders, 25 are cobblers, and 88 are yarn spinners. There are many others engaged in production. This point can be used to organize the following businesses: (1) Organize cooperatives with the aim of helping rickshaw pullers and small cart pullers, so that members are not exploited by the owners of the rickshaw companies. (2) Organize small-scale production cooperatives. The society can divide the work according to the needs of the members, such as making grass shoes, weaving reed curtains, threading toothbrushes, and spinning yarn. The purpose is to enable the products of family handicrafts or small crafts to be sold directly in the market, avoiding the exploitation of middlemen. At the same time, appropriate guidance should be given to improve their products and increase their income.

The Public Works Department Reviews Hotel and Restaurant Licenses 98

More than 40 Applicants Approved or Rejected Separately

The Public Works Department's Security Committee met on March 23rd to discuss the issue of hotels, restaurants, and other applications for licenses. The public was allowed to express their opposition to this issue. Therefore, Colonel Darby of the Salvation Army, representative of the Army and Navy YMCA Zhedeyin, and Dr. Barry attended on that day. Colonel Darby immediately expressed his opinion, saying that there are already many places selling alcohol, and he hopes that the committee will issue as few licenses as possible. Mr. Zhe and Mr. Barry also expressed their agreement with this opinion. The chairman of the committee then thanked the representatives and said that the Public Works Department's issuance of this type of license is based on the happiness and order of the community. Then, the review proceeded as follows: (A) Hotels: Applicants were: 1. No. 85 Shanxi Road, 2. No. 931 to No. 941 Jing'an Temple Road, 3. No. 95 to No. 101 Xihua Road. The first two locations were approved. The third location already had a restaurant license and wanted to apply for a hotel license so that it could sell alcohol outside of meal times. After consideration, it was considered that the location already had sufficient supply and was therefore rejected. (B) Taverns: Applicants were: 1. No. 8 Central Road and No. 15 Xinkang Road, 2. No. 11 and No. 13 Xinkang Road, 3. No. 61 Xizang Road, 4. No. 80 Xieqiao Road, 5. No. 431 Racecourse Road, 6. No. 19 Haining Road, 7. No. 145 Broadway Road. For the first, fifth, seventh, and third locations, the police considered that the locations already had sufficient supply and rejected them. The fourth location was temporarily approved, pending reports from all locations before approval. The remaining locations were approved. (C) Restaurants (selling alcohol only during meals): There were 15 applicants. Among them, No. 19 Guangdong Road, No. 233 Sichuan Road, and No. 99 Seymour Road, already had a considerable number of places selling alcohol, and the applications were approved without much discussion. No. 71 to No. 721 Jing'an Temple Road, this location was temporarily approved, pending reports from all locations before approval. No. 248A Broadway Road, this location was approved, but the license should state that only mild alcoholic beverages are allowed to be served during meals. No. 3 and No. 5 Yalv Road, someone protested this application. It was resolved to grant a temporary license, but not to disturb the neighboring houses, and to approve it after satisfactory reports from all locations. No. 9, Lane 44, Youheng Road, a temporary license was granted, pending further discussion after reports from all locations. The remaining locations, No. 577 to No. 583 Nanjing Road, No. 741 Jing'an Temple Road, No. 54, No. 55 Laoguan Road, No. 131 Bazilu, and No. 139 East Broadway Road, were all approved. (D) Sellers of beer and other malt liquors: There were 20 applicants, namely: 1. No. 104 Central Mansion, 2. No. 437 Guangxi Road, 3. No. 387 Nanjing Road, 4. No. 4 Kade Road, 5. No. 26 Shide Road, 6. No. 27 Shide Road, 7. No. 246 to No. 7 Mulming Road, 8. No. 70 Sun Avenue, 9. No. 12 Haining Road, 10. No. 34 Haining Road, 11. No. 1221 Hanbilu Road, 12. No. 138 Haining Road, 13. No. 807 North Sichuan Road, 14. No. 89 Kunshan Road, 15. No. 188 Kunshan Road, 16. No. 115 Bazilu, 17. No. 147 to No. 149 Xihua Road, 18. No. 82 to No. 83 Wusong Road, 19. No. 318 to No. 9 East Broadway Road, and No. 600A East Broadway Road. The first, ninth, and twelfth locations were rejected because there were already many supplies in those locations. The fifth location was rejected because it had not complied with the regulations of the Health Department. The sixth location was granted a temporary license, pending further review of reports from the Public Works Department and the Fire Department. The seventeenth location was granted a temporary license, pending reports from all locations for further review. The twentieth location was rejected because there were already many supplies there, and the police did not approve of granting a license. Later, someone explained that the store owner depended on this for a living, and if he could not sell beer, the income would not be enough. Therefore, he asked the bureau to grant a temporary license for one year, which would surely satisfy the police. The chief of police then stated that there were many similar situations, and if this precedent was set, it would be impossible to refuse others in the future. Therefore, the committee rejected it. All other applicants were approved. In addition, licenses that had already been issued and were renewed in accordance with the regulations were also approved. The committee's decision was submitted to the Board of Directors on the 29th and adopted by the Board of Directors.

Vaccination Certificates to Charge Handling Fees 109

The head of the Public Health Department of the Public Works Department reported that doctors in this office had vaccinated the staff of a certain company, and the company now requests that vaccination certificates be issued by name. It is found that this type of certificate has always been issued upon request and has never been charged a fee. However, in order to protect the business of practicing physicians, it is proposed to charge a handling fee for this type of certificate, which seems to be beneficial to all parties. This proposal was considered by the Health Committee, which considered it appropriate to charge a small handling fee. Therefore, it was decided that a fee of two yuan per person would be charged for this type of certificate in the future, and the head of the Public Health Department could consider waiving the fee for the poor. This case has been submitted to the Board of Directors and has been approved for implementation.

Hudong Residents' Refusal to Cut Off Water Supply: Absolutely Denying Water Rate Increase 110

The United Committee of Hudong District Residents Refusing Water Cut-off, based on the resolution of yesterday's emergency meeting, sent letters to the Real Estate Association, the Chinese Directors of the Municipal Council, and Mr. Feng Bingnan, expressing their positions. The contents are recorded as follows:

To the Real Estate Association:

Greetings. We believe you have received and reviewed our letter sent on March 25th. Having read in the newspapers that the water fee issue, with a one-third increase before March, has been reluctantly paid by your association for relief, we are deeply grateful for your public spirit. However, according to reports from representatives of Balfour Apartments, Barlow Apartments, Shuncheng Apartments, Sanyuan Lane, etc., the water pipes there have not yet been properly installed. We ask that you promptly consult with the owners to find a solution so that the situation can be restored as soon as possible. Our committee absolutely denies any increase in water fees, and we hope that your association will continue its original intention and work hard to negotiate to achieve a satisfactory outcome. Our committee will follow your lead and pledge to be your strong support.

To the Chinese Directors of the Municipal Council:

Greetings. The British-owned Water Company's increase in water fees and illegal water cut-offs have caused immense suffering to the citizens who bear the brunt of the impact. Considering the company's vicious intentions and harsh measures, it seems determined to put our citizens to death. All Chinese people share a deep sense of indignation. Our committee has therefore contacted the residents of the Eastern District to form the United Committee Refusing Water Cut-off, and, along with the Real Estate Association, has appealed to all parties. The situation has been reported extensively in the newspapers, and we believe it is already well-known. Although the Real Estate Association and mediators have negotiated a temporary transitional solution, paying an additional one-third of the original water package rate for relief up to the end of February, this transitional solution is merely a temporary fix. Since the January 28th Incident, all industries have been depressed, and the economy has reached a low point. Citizens cannot afford to bear any additional burden. Moreover, according to the Water Company's business report on March 30th, it has a surplus profit, making the price increase unnecessary. It is evident that there is an intention to mistreat the common people. We look to you, the directors, to shoulder the important responsibility entrusted by the citizens, and we hope that you will argue reasonably, overturn the water meter system, and restore the original state to maintain the livelihood of the common people and alleviate public suffering. We would be deeply grateful.

To Mr. Feng Bingnan:

We have long admired your demeanor and deeply yearn for your leadership. This water cut-off issue has caused a serious situation. We are deeply grateful for your enthusiasm for public welfare, your efforts in mediation, and the temporary relief obtained. The residents of this district are grateful for your efforts. However, we hope that you will continue to work hard to find a fundamental solution to eliminate public suffering. It would be like saving the lives of countless families.

Guanghua Company Denies Price War with Russian Oil 112

National Monthly Sales of 300,000 Gallons

Plan to Increase Gas Stations to 50

The Continental Daily News reports that the Guanghua Company, which sells Russian oil in China, denied yesterday that it intended to engage in a price war with companies such as Socony and Asiatic Petroleum. However, it stated that it has a large-scale plan to develop its business in Shanghai and throughout the country. It is said that the company's gasoline price is also one dollar and five cents per U.S. gallon, the same as the prices of Socony, Asiatic Petroleum, and Texaco. However, the actual selling price can be reduced by five cents for regular customers, and even more for bulk purchases. Currently, the company only has two gas stations in Shanghai, one at 1089 Foch Road and the other near the Nanjing Grand Theatre on Edward VII Avenue. It plans to add 50 more in the two concessions and the north and south cities. Fifty pumps ordered from the United States are expected to arrive this week. Many locations for installation have also been purchased, and construction will begin as soon as approval is obtained from the authorities. The company will do its best to complete the work as soon as possible for the convenience of users. Currently, the company sells approximately 300,000 gallons of gasoline per month nationwide, which is six times more than in the second half of last year. However, compared to the largest competitors, which sell over one million gallons per month, it is still far behind. In addition, the company is also competing fiercely with British and American companies in the kerosene market. Normally, it sells approximately three million gallons per month, but due to the price war among competitors, sales are not reaching that number. It currently has two oil storage facilities in Shanghai, one in Pudong and one in Gaoqiao, and has no plans to add any more for the time being. However, it is currently constructing new storage facilities in Hankou and other major cities in the interior.

Communist Party Secret Communication Method 113

White Cotton Cloth with Willow Pattern Found in Chen Shuying's Residence

Writing Discovered on the Cloth Surface After Chemical Testing

Detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Police, in cooperation with detectives from the Public Concession, arrested Chen Guang, commander of the Red Army, and his sister, Chen Shuying, for investigation. The police have now chemically tested the white cotton cloth with a willow pattern found in Chen Shuying's residence at 290 Rue Mabilais. Surprisingly, the moment the chemical solution touched the cloth, writing appeared on the surface. This is a method used by the Communist Party for secret communication. Yesterday afternoon, the case was also heard by the Second Higher Branch of the court. The Western detective demonstrated the chemical testing procedure in court. Subsequently, Judge Yu concluded the interrogation and ordered that Chen Guang and Chen Shuying, along with the evidence, be sent to the Shanghai Municipal Police for further interrogation.

Where Did the Scrap Iron in West Shanghai Come From? The Public is Investigating 114

During the past week, many piles of scrap iron were suddenly discovered on a vacant lot at the intersection of Caojiadu Wujiaochang and Bailinan Road in West Shanghai. Capture of Inland Kidnappers Under Investigation 115

Total of Twelve Men and Women – Further Interrogation Scheduled After Investigation

The Shanghai Municipal Police received a report that a gang of kidnappers who had repeatedly committed kidnapping for ransom in Kunshan, Qingpu, and other places had fled to Shanghai after hiding the kidnapped victims in Benniu Town, Changzhou. They were hiding at 291 Binlang Road in the Public Concession. Therefore, at 4:30 yesterday morning, detectives were dispatched to the Putuo Road Police Station to request assistance in apprehending the criminals. The head of the police station dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to the address. Upon arrival, the building was dark and all the men, women, old and young, upstairs and downstairs, were awakened from their dreams. Because the detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Police did not initially specify the names of the criminals involved in the kidnapping case, all the occupants of the building were arrested, totaling twelve men and women. Among them were Hao Ziming, Hao Lihong, Hao Lifeng, and Ziming's sisters Chen Hao and Wang Hao, as well as their sister Qian Chen Jingqing and nephew Chen Jingfa, all from Jiangbei. The others were Chen Yushan, a 68-year-old man from Anhui, Chen Shengfan, 52 years old, and Chen Yushan's daughter-in-law Chen Zhao and relative Wang Yu, a total of four people. In addition, there was Zhang Xianghua from Hangzhou. The detectives also found a pistol and 51 bullets under the bed in Chen Yushan's bedroom and brought them back to the police station for separate detention. At 9 o'clock, they were transferred to the First Special District Local Court, where Magistrate Qian Wenji conducted a preliminary hearing. The detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Police presented an official letter requesting that all the arrested men and women be transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Police for interrogation. However, the police lawyer Wang Yaotang objected, stating that the arrest of these people had not proven who was involved in the kidnapping. If everyone were to be taken away immediately, it would be a serious violation of the Public Concession authorities' intention to protect law-abiding citizens. He requested that everyone be detained for investigation by the police station and that the Shanghai Municipal Police should provide sufficient evidence to prove who the kidnappers were and whether all the men and women were criminals to avoid injustice. Magistrate Qian briefly questioned Hao Ziming and others one by one and ordered them to be temporarily detained separately, pending further investigation and interrogation.

Judgment in the Zhou Xiangyun Accusation of Abduction Case 116

Zhou Xiangyun, a wealthy Ningbo businessman, met Wu Yue'e, a prostitute from Dongtingshan working in a brothel named Longyu in 1915. Soon, they rented a house at 100 Qinshou Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, and lived together. However, in recent years, Zhou suddenly abandoned Wu and treated her as a stranger, refusing to provide her with living expenses. Although Wu visited him to negotiate, he refused to see her. He also refused to reply to her letters. Wu then hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the First Court, accusing Zhou of abduction and abandonment. After the First Court summoned Zhou several times, Zhou claimed that he had never met Wu and had never seen her before. How could there be such a thing as abduction? Wu presented Zhu, the landlady of Qinshou Lane, to testify in court that Wu and Zhou did live together until 1927. After the debate was concluded, Chief Judge Feng Shide of the Criminal Division of the First Court announced the judgment yesterday morning: Zhou Xiangyun was acquitted.

169th Report on the Four Banks Issuance Reserve 117

Reader Consultant

Further Discussion on "Supply Power and Western Civilization" 120

Letter from Mr. Xu Xianfu of this city (1)

Mr. Reporter: The letter I hastily replied to on March 2nd amidst busy school affairs was actually published in your esteemed newspaper on the 14th. This letter has raised many questions from you, which you want me to answer. I will now answer them separately. (1) This is your insightful point (3) from your reply on the 14th, which I will address first. The meaning of "feeling" in psychology is that "感" (gan, feeling) is the feeling received from a stimulus (Stimulus), and "慨" (kai, lament/emotion) is Response. The "feeling" in my first letter (published on February 28th) was a kind of strong "emotion" arising from the accumulated "feelings" of the past. Therefore, it was both lengthy and agitated, and I trespassed on your esteemed space. "Research" in English is Research, which is searching for the desired purpose from the environment or materials. This kind of work also happens after a wave of emotion. James believed that the human "self" is composed of three parts: material, social, and spiritual. We often have feelings of satisfaction and dissatisfaction towards the expression of these three parts, and thus the so-called "self-awareness" arises. I think this step is equivalent to "feeling." James also said that our satisfaction and dissatisfaction with self-awareness lead to physical self-seeking, social self-seeking, and spiritual self-seeking. I believe this is the work of research. Understanding this, then feeling and research are different. And the feeling in my first letter was not venting a pre-existing concept related to the survival of the country and the rise and fall of the nation, but rather associating it with the country and the nation after the venting, so I requested publication. But, please do not despise it as feeling, feeling is also related to the country and the nation. For example, Xiang Ji, seeing the awesome power of the King of Qin, exclaimed, "I can take his place!" Later, he led eight thousand men across the river. Ban Chao, working as a government scribe, threw down his pen and sighed! "A real man has no other ambitions, he should also emulate Fu Jiezi and Zhang Qian in establishing merit in foreign lands to be granted a title and land, how can he be confined to writing forever!" Therefore, he opened up the Western Regions. Emperor Taizu of Song drunkenly said to Shi Shouxin and others, "If someone puts a yellow robe on you, even if you don't want it, can you avoid it!" The next day, Shouxin and others begged to resign from the command of the imperial guards. Thus, the military power was relinquished over a cup of wine. Sakyamuni witnessed the inequality of Indian society and felt deeply, saying, "If I don't go to hell, who will go to hell." What was its impact on India and China later? Socialist pioneer Fourier, in 1799, happened to be a clerk in a rice store. The owner ordered him to throw the rotten rice into the sea in order to increase the price of rice. Fourier immediately deeply felt the sin of this kind of commercial capitalism and rose up to reform society. Fichte, angered by Germany's being trampled by Napoleon, after the Battle of Jena (1808), used ardent emotions to publish his Address to the German Nation. What was the impact of this article on the fate of Germany? Here, it should be stated that Fu is also incompetent, how dare he compare himself to the sages, but just cite a few examples. If there is something Mr. doesn't approve of in me, I hope you don't disapprove of the sages because of it! (2) Here, let's discuss the supply power and Western civilization. In China and in the West, "nature" is equally invasive, which Mr. also admits. May I ask, how does China control the difficulties of nature? In a word, it is helpless. For example, the active national wealth cannot be exploited, the national land is inconvenient for transportation, and the passive ones, such as the Yellow River, cannot prevent or provide relief for floods. But Western civilization is not like this, it can stop and overcome nature and can also use it to supply people with the knowledge and technology of evolution (it is said that a German engineer used an artificial Yellow River to study the Yellow River's water conservancy, why doesn't China have it), this is the difference between Eastern and Western civilizations, that is, the characteristic of Western civilization, calling it the essence, who says it is not appropriate! Then the two sentences in my first and second letters are both true, and not one is true and one is false. In a capitalist environment, in a socialist environment, "nature" is also equally invasive, which is also admitted by Mr. But Mr. believes that there are also differences in the supply power between capitalism and socialism, because "conquering nature is carried out in human society." This sentence, I think, accidentally puts the cart before the horse, because human society is carried out in the human conquest of nature. Historical facts tell us, no need to seek it in ancient times, the emergence of modern capitalism, after the industrial revolution in the late 18th century, is after the technological progress of human control and utilization of nature. The world competition of imperialism began after Darwin's theory of evolution of "survival of the fittest", that is, after the intellectual progress of human overcoming of nature. Even in the current Soviet Union, her knowledge and technology of conquering nature, which one is not quoted by capitalist countries! Such as American engineers, German machinery, etc. Her socialist society, in terms of knowledge and technology 丨丨 The power of supply is not completely different from capitalist society, but the direction of applying knowledge and technology is different. What Mr. said, has the adjectives "planned, systematic, most economical, and most fully", which only expresses the characteristics of the direction of the socialist dominance of the quantity, in other words, like the Soviet socialist country, her application of human knowledge and technology tends to the direction of "planned, systematic, most economical, and most fully". Dr. Walter W. Lucasse of the United States said: "They (pure scientists) handed over knowledge to society, and society should be fully responsible for whether it uses it properly or improperly." Then why don't we say that capitalism's application of evolutionary knowledge and technology is improper, and socialism's application of evolutionary knowledge and technology is proper, which depends on how we control and dominate society? It has nothing to do with the power of supply. This is why Britain, Germany, and the United States are Britain, Germany, and the United States, and the Soviet Union is the Soviet Union. So what I said "the difference between capitalism and socialism lies only in the power of guiding the direction of human evolution" does not lose half of the true content. (3) Here, I will reply to Mr. Fourteen's point (2) again. Regarding this point, Mr. seems to have a misunderstanding in my first letter. I dare to say that Mr.'s misunderstanding is that he thinks the main body of that letter is the public health problem. In fact, I feel the fanaticism and wasteful danger and unsuitability of sports among some of our country's rulers and so-called leaders, as well as some young people and urban people. From those accumulated stimuli, it was fully released in the most recent and stronger stimuli, and this kind of aversion chained other aversions, that is, from feeling that sports is not the way out of China to associating that the way out of China lies in saving the foolish. The proposal of military training and productive labor to alleviate health problems is just a step back, this can be reviewed. Since Mr. has this misunderstanding, the five questions raised are also aimed at solving the health problem. In fact, they are the whole way out for them (workers and peasants), finding their way out is also finding China's way out. And whether Chinese society will be under the power of capitalist dominance or the power of socialist dominance also depends on this. As for Mr.'s point (4), I don't need to say much about the difference between capitalism and socialism, because Mr. himself has answered for me above. What's more, the sages and pioneers in history have pointed out to us, and the Soviet Union and other countries have divided for us in fact. Finally, I express regret for the fact that the words in the last letter were more than the meaning! But I don't know what about this letter?

We believe that although newspaper reports are based on the principle of recording everything heard, but before the case is adjudicated, the right and wrong are not yet clear, the newspaper should not make a big hue and cry, so as to make a one-sided propaganda and damage the reputation of others. Therefore, we have entrusted your lawyer to represent them and send a letter to the newspaper, requesting correction, etc. We hereby inform you accordingly, hoping that you will investigate and correct it quickly. Education News

Important News

Jiangsu Education Department Strictly Handles the Handover of County Education Directors 124

▲ Former Rugao Education Director Summoned to the Province

丨Has Been Released on Bail to Borrow Money丨

Since Director Zhou of the Jiangsu Education Department took office, he has attached great importance to the handover of education directors in various counties. Since the 16th year of the Republic, there have been more than 170 cases of new and old education directors in various counties who have not completed the handover or have not even handled the handover. The department has been actively managing since last winter, repeatedly ordering the previous and current education directors to complete the handover within a time limit, strictly checking and auditing the numbers. As of now, dozens of counties have been processed, and the rest are being processed. It is heard that all can be cleared this summer vacation. Recently, the former Director of the Rugao County Education Bureau, Rui Jiarui, handled the receipt and expenditure of education fees totaling more than 1.5 million yuan. After the handover, the bureau submitted the director's accounts to the Economic Audit Committee for review. As a result, it was found that the amount of extravagant expenses and amounts without formal receipts reached 40,000 yuan. The county government submitted the review forms to the Education Department for approval. The Education Department instructed the former director to go to the Rugao Education Bureau for accounting on March 1st and sent personnel to supervise the audit. Unexpectedly, the former director did not go to Rugao at the appointed time. The supervisors summoned the county director and representatives of the Economic Audit Committee to conduct a detailed audit of the review forms. It was determined that the extravagance was indeed extravagant, and those that should be deleted totaled more than 11,000 yuan. A list was prepared and jointly submitted to the Education Department. The Education Department believed that the former director's extravagance during his tenure had been clearly audited by the supervisors and should be strictly recovered to emphasize special funds. The Education Department immediately presented it to the provincial government and sent officials to Nanjing to verify the former director's residence and summon him to the province to calculate the list and send a copy to the former director, ordering him to clarify and reply. After further verification, in addition to ordering the bureau to review the various amounts, it was calculated that more than 4,000 yuan should be paid first, and he was instructed to raise the money and hand it over immediately. The former director could not raise money in the department and sought the Nanjing Xinli Construction Company and Gongxing Coal Company as guarantors, and the principal of a certain private school in Nanjing jointly guaranteed to bear 1,000 yuan of responsibility. The Education Department has now approved the bail to go out to raise money. Furthermore, those former education directors in various counties who have outstanding public funds that have not been supplemented as ordered, and a few who have delayed and disobeyed the order to handle the handover, will be requested to be wanted and transferred to the court for handling according to law.

University Education Joint Association Issues Declaration on Academic Nation-Saving 127

▲ Improve Scientific Equipment to Create a Cultural Environment ▲ Promote Advanced Research and Popularize National Education

The Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff in Shanghai previously resolved to issue a declaration on academic nation-saving. The second standing committee meeting appointed Chen Jilie to jointly review with the original drafter Kang Xuanyi. Chairman Zhang Shouyong made the final amendments and signed and sent the telegram. The original telegram is transcribed as follows:

Public gong to all levels of schools, cultural institutions, and academic groups in the country. A nation exists in the world, and it must have a foundation for its existence. What is it? It lies in academics. Tracing back to history, verifying recent events, and examining how France was able to recover after defeat, and how Germany was able to survive even though it was divided, the fundamental basis for its recovery and survival is nothing else, but the prosperity of academics. Our country has inherited thousands of years of culture. Not only does everyone have characteristics, but even in terms of science, there have been creations and inventions throughout the dynasties. It is only because we are content with simplicity, lose our spirit, and do not seek progress that we are bewildered and fall behind. The violent therefore take advantage of it, regardless of the world's trends, and are completely contrary to the world's trends. And we Chinese reflect on ourselves, there are hundreds of ways to get sick, but there is only one way to win. Why is the countryside bankrupt? Why are factories dilapidated? Why does commercial warfare fail? And why can't education be popularized? Why is morality declining day by day? All are the harms of not emphasizing academics. Therefore, saving the country lies only in academics. If academics prosper, then farmers, workers, and merchants will all get its guidance. In peacetime, it is beneficial to politics, and in wartime, it is beneficial to the military. And mechanical precision and convenient transportation are all embodied in this. At this time of serious national crisis, we should take actively resisting violent Japan as the current palliative measure, and take promoting academics as the fundamental plan for saving the country. This has been resolved by the general meeting to take April 1st as the total mobilization of the national education community, that is, to take academic nation-saving as the period for jointly going to the national crisis. From this day on, we will unanimously base on this meaning, work hard together to improve scientific equipment, create a cultural environment, promote advanced research, popularize national education, enrich the elements of establishing a country, and complete spiritual construction and material construction. Do not advocate empty talk, do not seek quick results, use three years of wormwood to cure seven years of disease, mend the fold after the sheep is lost, the mulberry elm has not yet fallen, and saving the crisis depends on this. As for the detailed plan for academic nation-saving, the colleagues of this association have shallow academic positions, and are deeply afraid of not contributing to the advanced. I hope that the gentlemen will express their great opinions and give guidance so that we can follow the path. We hereby send our connections first, and we will wait for your enlightenment. The United Association of Faculty and Staff of Shanghai Universities kowtows.

Sports Hall Opening Ceremony 132

At 10:00 AM, the opening ceremony of the Fook Kai Seen Sports Hall was held. More than 500 guests arrived. After the ceremony was held as scheduled, President Li reported first, briefly stating that school education, moral education, intellectual education, group education, and physical education are equally important. Our school has always paid attention to physical education. In the spring of the 29th year of Guangxu during the late Qing Dynasty, it created the sports meeting as the pioneer of various schools. Afterwards, it has been held every year, up to now for 30 years. However, there are still many deficiencies in terms of equipment. After I became the president of the school, I considered this and planned to build and expand this field. The project started in July of the 19th year of the Republic of China and lasted for two years and eight months to this day. The construction cost is about 10,000 yuan. The entire field covers an area of 40 mu and has become the latest type of sports field with a width of 8 meters and a circle of 400 meters. Outside, there is a 200-meter straight track. The land inside the track is also used as a football field and military training field. If cement grandstands can be built around it in the future, it can become a complete sports field. This field is named Fook Kai Seen to commemorate the pioneer Dr. Fook Kai Seen. Dr. Fook Kai Seen served as the supervisor of this school for four years during the establishment period of the school, building school buildings and managing education affairs. He also carefully studied Chinese studies and vigorously promoted physical education. His promotion of merit has reached the country, and it is not only what the colleagues of this school should be grateful for. I deeply hope that the younger generation of students will come to this field and recall Dr. Fook Kai Seen's deep meaning of promoting physical education, and never forget the spirit of this school to promote physical education, strengthen the body to strengthen the species, and reach others by reaching themselves, etc. Then Mrs. Decker, daughter of Fook Kai Seen, gave the opening speech, briefly saying that it is very happy to participate in the opening ceremony of the Fook Kai Seen Sports Hall of your school today. I am especially honored that your school named the field after my father's name. I deeply hope that all the students can use this good sports field to increase the health of each person's physique. Finally, he apologized on behalf of Fook Kai Seen for not being able to come and participate, etc. Then Dr. Wang Zhengting gave a speech, briefly saying that 37 years ago, this place was called Nanyang, and it is still deeply imprinted in my mind. In the past, it was not easy to start new schools and introduce Western culture to the East, so there were very few schools. Your school was able to start in a difficult environment, and this cannot but be attributed to Mr. Fook Kai Seen. Furthermore, in the beginning, schools focused on knowledge and character, and did not pay attention to health at all, but Mr. Fu had a broad vision and worked hard to promote it. Nanyang's ability to have today's glory in sports cannot but be attributed to Mr. Fook Kai Seen. Now I encourage you with the word "constant". We should not have a five-minute heat, we must have a permanent heat, etc. Finally, the Public Security Bureau Military Band played music and the ceremony was completed.

Student Army Grand Review 133

At 11:00 AM, the student army drill and review of all students in the first and second years was held. Ji Lue assumed the role of general commander. First, there was a march-past, and then a review of the troops. We should work hard and strive to practice the word "constant". Military training should especially follow this word "constant" and practice diligently.

Sino-British International Billiards Competition

China Wins First Championship 139

China Wins a Total of 834 Points After Five Days, Li Gongying Defeats Bernal

(Final Battle): Unfavorable in the First Half, Major Victory in the Second Half, Score is 1000 Points to 776 Points

In the Sino-British international billiards competition, after five days of competition, China won a total of 834 points, securing the first championship. The five Chinese representatives in this competition each made significant contributions; it was not the effort of just one or two people. In the final battle yesterday, China's "Billiards King" Li Gongying faced the renowned British veteran Bernal. Li was at a disadvantage in the first half, but turned defeat into victory in the second half. As a result, Li scored 1000 points to Bernal's 776 points, creating a record of China winning four out of five matches. The Yong'an Company and Mr. Li Minzhou of the Xin Xin Company each presented silver cups, engraved with the names of the victors, to be kept permanently at the Bank Club as a lasting memorial.

Performing Well in Favorable Circumstances 140

The performance of the leading players from both countries was not as exceptional as their usual peak performance. Li had some inconsistencies, while Bernal was more seasoned and steady. In the first ten shots, Li had a slight advantage, 105 to 92. After another five shots, Bernal took the lead. After another five shots, they were even again. By the thirty-fifth shot, Bernal was ahead by 64 points. Soon, Li gradually improved. By the forty-sixth shot, Li was behind by as many as 100 points. Before long, Bernal, finding himself in a favorable situation, performed exceptionally well, scoring continuously, adding up to 497 points. With only three more points needed to finish the first half, the old general showed great vigor in his old age but suddenly held back six times, giving Li the opportunity to make a final move. Unfortunately, Li did not gain much, and Bernal finished the 500 points at 442.

Using Skill to Turn Defeat into Victory 141

The situation in the second half was completely different. After the fifth shot at the start, Bernal scored 52 points, but there were no other special achievements. Li, after scores of 40 and 56, brought the two sides to a level playing field. At the fifteenth shot, the opponent's ball had fallen into the hole, the red ball was near the bottom edge, and the cue ball was on the left side. With no direct path to hit the red ball, Li used a skillful technique, touching the red ball and circling around it, falling into the hole on its own. The spectators were amazed and applauded. After this ball was made, Li continuously hit the red ball and made the cue ball fall into the hole 18 times, scoring 59 points. From then on, he turned defeat into victory. At the thirty-fifth shot, he made many consecutive "ma balls," scoring 71 points. Soon after, he scored another 45 points, and the victory was secured. The final result was 1000 points to 776 points.

(Right) Silver cups presented by Mr. Li Minzhou of Xin Xin Company (above) and Yong'an Company (below) (Left) (1) Li Gongying, (2) Shen Lince, (3) Zhang Yingda, (4) Liu Fuzong, (5) Xu Shizhang

Evaluating the Players' Skills 142

The five-day competition has been detailed in this newspaper in recent days. There are noteworthy aspects of the individual skills of the five Chinese players. On the Chinese side, Li Gongying has yet to fully demonstrate his capabilities, but his several comebacks from seemingly impossible situations were truly beyond the reach of ordinary people. Shen Lince has made much progress, showing versatility. Zhang Yingda has a firm grip on his shots, making them freely and easily. Liu Fuzong's skills are inherently excellent, but he has been unlucky. Xu Shizhang is bold, meticulous, and skillful with his hands. Among the five British players, Bernal is known for his experience, McShell and Nema exert their utmost effort, Baker has moments of incredible skill, and Marx suffers from stage fright.

Disciplinary Action in Middle School Basketball Tournament: Nanshang Suspended for One Year 147

Improper Conduct Deserves Severe Punishment; Guanghua Players Receive Warning

Emergency Resolution by the Middle School Sports Federation Yesterday

The Shanghai Middle School Sports Federation held an emergency meeting yesterday morning at the Sports Advancement Association to discuss the basketball dispute between Guanghua and Nanshang on the 28th of last month. The attendees included Wu Lisheng from Shangzhong, Zhang Xi'en from Chizhi, Zhang Kan from Pudong, Mao Sucen, Wu Yuru, and Wu Zhongkang from Nanshang, Chen Bingde and Zeng Hanmo from Fushi, Han Kuiyong from Fuzhong (also representing Minli), Shen Meizhen from Daxia, Lu Xiangqian from Guanghua, Peng Sanmei from Hujiang, and basketball committee members Zhang Wugao and Dong Xiaopei, totaling fifteen people. First, the referee's report from that day and a letter from the Guanghua basketball team were distributed to the attendees. Then, Zhang Wugao was elected as the temporary chairman. During the discussion of the disciplinary measures, the representatives from Nanshang and Guanghua left the meeting. The full text of the resolution is published below:

According to the reports from the referee and the staff present at the venue, during the basketball championship game between Nanyang Commercial High School and Guanghua High School on the 28th of last month, held at the Zhonghua Basketball Hall, students and cheerleaders from Nanshang rushed onto the court and beat Guanghua players. This conduct was extremely improper and deserves severe punishment to maintain discipline and serve as a warning to others. Therefore, it was resolved to suspend Nanyang Commercial High School from all sports competitions in the Federation for one year (from April 1933 to March 1934). After the suspension period, the school authorities must provide a firm guarantee before being allowed to participate in competitions again. During the first year after rejoining, it will be a probationary period. If any further improper behavior is discovered, the school's membership will be immediately revoked. The game in question will be considered a forfeit by Nanshang, and Guanghua will be declared the winner. As for the Guanghua basketball team, their players' actions in this season's games have been less than satisfactory and should be warned to emphasize sportsmanship.

Large Number of Sign-Ups for Long-Distance Race 148

Important Information for Long-Distance Race Participants 149

1. Starting Point: Gather and register near the Chen Yingshi Memorial Tower at the Old West Gate before starting.

2. Finishing Point: March straight in front of the Public Works Bureau on City Hall Road.

3. Route: From the Chen Yingshi Memorial Tower, head north along Minguo Road and Zhonghua Road to the Small West Gate, then head west along Daxing Street, Dalin Road, Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road, Xietu Road, and Xiaomuqiao Road, then head north to City Hall Road, arriving at the front gate of the Public Works Bureau.

4. Distance: The entire distance is divided into ten stages, with each stage being one kilometer, marked with Arabic numerals 12345678910.

5. Award Ceremony Location: Athletes should rest at the Public Works Bureau after reaching the finishing point. After all athletes have arrived, the referee will lead them to the City Hall to participate in the award ceremony.

6. Race Rules: During the race, participants must strictly follow the route set by the organizers. If a participant runs off course, they must return to the point where they went off course and resume running. Participants must not step onto the sidewalk, receive assistance, or obstruct other athletes.

7. Athletes should inform their caretakers to bring their changes of clothes to the open space inside the gate of the Public Works Bureau in advance. They are not allowed to accompany the athletes along the race route or disrupt the order.

Publication of "German Revival Gymnastics" 152

▲ Germany Revitalizes Itself with Ateur Holger's Gymnastics

丨China Can Also Use This to Strengthen the Nation to Resist Japan

The sports series published by Shanghai Qin Fen Bookstore has already published more than forty titles and has long been praised by the sports community throughout the country. It is now heard that the bookstore has published "German Revival Gymnastics." The original author is the renowned German sports expert, Mr. Ateur Holger. Seeing the decline in the spirit of the German people after the defeat in the war, Mr. Holger created these gymnastics to promote the revival of the German nation. Several years later, it indeed achieved great results. Now, our country should use this method of training as a reference. Therefore, Qin Fen Bookstore invited sports experts Pei Xiyuan and Lu Xiangqian to translate this book into Chinese, so that the Chinese people can adopt it concretely. The whole book is divided into eighty-four sections, including "upper limbs," "lower limbs," "body," "swinging," "bending," "squatting," "head," "correction," "abdomen," "waist," "balance," "jumping," and "mimicking." Each section is accompanied by clear illustrations, making it easy for readers to understand. The entire book is priced at five jiao, with a special price of 10% off. An additional three fen is charged for postage to other locations, and eight fen for registration. The general distributor is at 392 Father Rhodes Road, French Concession, Shanghai, and the store is at 554 Sima Road, British Concession, Shanghai.
