Essays

April's Wine and Fish 156

— Zhanlu

丨Willing to Drink April 7th Wine丨丨Do Not Be an April 1st Fish丨

The weather in April is perfect for spring outings! Especially for the spring vacation tour groups between Six Bridges and Three Temples, enjoying the leisurely life of ascending buildings to drink wine and watching fish by the water; however, expanding the panoramic view of the world, I am willing to drink America's April 7th wine, but not be Europe's April 1st fish.

Since the wets succumbed to the dries, the American people have not been able to drink their fill of alcoholic beverages for thirteen years! Fortunately, after Roosevelt took office, he first relaxed the prohibition of distilled spirits; from one minute past midnight on April 7th, the average New World alcoholic could freely drink his fill! The opening of the liquor ban, which has been buzzing for years, only had the possibility of realization in April; no wonder the day the president was inaugurated, the large liquor barrel strutted its stuff in the parade. I can imagine the American alcoholics, whose mouths have been parched, pouring cup after cup into the liquor urns that have been dry for thirteen years, which is called being willing to drink America's April 7th wine.

April 1st is April Fool's Day, and people in various European countries take pleasure in fooling others on this day; in English custom, anyone who is fooled on this day is called an April fool. In Scottish custom, the person who is fooled is called an April cuckoo, and they often throw a game letter at people, saying:

On the first of April, strike the cuckoo in the wood of another mountain.

The receiver often replies:

The cuckoo and the skylark roost in the same tree... I am the same as both of you, I am a cuckoo, and you are also cuckoos.

In French custom, the person who is fooled on this day is called an April fish; why is he called a fish? It is said that April is the birth season of fish, and young fish are often easily deceived; therefore, the fool is the April fish. We have the idiom "fish and meat countrymen," meaning the deceived countrymen can also be called fish, but there is no mention of April, and they are almost fish who are deceived for life! The fish that Europeans talk about being deceived is only accidentally a fish on April 1st, and after this day, he is no longer a fish, which is called not being an April 1st fish of Europe.

The Yellow Peril 157

— Yongzi

The yellow race conquered half of Europe, and even now Europeans still use this event to scare children. As a member of the yellow race, I am fortunate enough to have lived this life.

I have heard that the conquest of half of Europe by the yellow race is not only frightening to children in Europe, but even adults over fifty years old are praying to God day and night like blind people fearing the collapse of the sky, not to catch the sleeping bug in the nose of the sleeping lion of the East, otherwise, it is said that the "yellow peril" will engulf the entire earth.

Since conquering half of Europe, the sleeping lion of the East has been accumulating virtue, sleeping all the time, without eating a single white person, and it seems that it will not move a step until the hunters have tied it up tightly before it yawns. This situation can be considered as a dose of peace of mind for the white race.

Things are not easy to predict. The lion is sleeping sweetly, but the skinny yellow dog next to it is getting fatter and fatter, and more and more fierce. At first, it only nibbled at the lion's claws, but the year before last it simply swallowed the lion's tail. Recently, the yellow dog has become even more like it's gone mad, barking wildly at any shadow it sees.

The white race knows that the sleeping lion will not wake up for a while, and is happily planning to arrange it, but now it is dominated by the mad yellow dog, not allowing them to approach the sleeping lion. Watching the yellow dog swallow the lion's tail and gradually nibble at its belly, they suddenly remembered the "yellow peril" that Europeans talked about, which actually fell on the yellow dog.

The yellow dog, one day after eating the sleeping lion, will have an ever-growing appetite, and when it's hungry, it will easily swallow a white person in one bite, without leaving even bone fragments. At that time, "yellow" will truly become a "peril," which I am afraid will not only be used to scare children. I, side-by-side with the yellow dog with the word yellow, am grateful, grateful, take the opportunity, take the opportunity.

Milk 158

— Zheng Chuyao

The mere writing of that thought-provoking word "milk" immediately brings to mind tender white breasts, the two rounded hemispheres bulging to the left and right, like white jade; the mysterious apexes of the hemispheres, dotted with purplish-red lotus seeds, resembling two intoxicating fresh flowers, still in bud. Seated in a comfortable sofa, the warm sunlight basking one into a sleepy stupor, closing one’s eyes and thinking of this, one would feel the joy of a drunken man!

In my hometown of Hangzhou, the value of a woman’s breasts can be divided into three stages: the breasts of a maiden are cast from gold, because they are hidden inside a small vest, as precious as gold, not easily displayed for others' enjoyment; the breasts of a young married woman, they seem not as precious as gold? It is said that they are forged from silver, because they cannot belong solely to the woman forever as those of a maiden; a young woman’s breasts, half of the time they belong to her beloved husband. But, though this is said, aside from her husband, this charm will not be revealed; however, it is no longer as precious as gold! Only the woman who has already given birth to a child, in my hometown, they are called "dog grandma," because they no longer have the mystery of the maiden or young woman! In front of anyone, she would unashamedly pull out her breasts, once called gold and silver, to feed her child; it is like dog milk, belonging to the public! It is like a plaster model that can be admired by the public! It has lost the magical power that once made people fascinated and incredulous.

Venus Night 159

— Guo Lanxin

My heart filled with desolate and sorrowful spring night, I could not overcome the loneliness invading the small building, so I left my residence and walked alone towards the Venus Café, stepping into the small door illuminated by neon lights, I heard a burst of mournful music, and rushed into it amid the mournful rhythms.

The dim green light nurtured the joys and sorrows of the world. Here, there are endless laughter, buried sorrows, and exotic atmosphere. In a dimly lit corner, I ordered a bottle of Shanghai beer, sitting silently, as if leaving my troubled homeland, watching many foreign children dancing wildly, singing merrily, whispering sweet nothings, confiding in honeyed tones, but I did not know a single person, sitting alone drinking bitter beer, this is still the territory of my great China!

At the top four corners of this dance hall hung four glass lanterns riddled with holes, emitting five-colored light that swirled around, scattering disordered rays from the holes, like ghostly eyes, like divine lamps, making you dazed and turned into a colorblind person.

I opened my eyes and looked around, there were Anglo-Saxons, Slavs, Japanese, and also a Han Chinese like me, holding sorrows of my great China, this place seems like an international café.

Many sailors drunkenly embraced slender waists while dancing, scantily dressed foreign dancers, half-naked in thin spring clothes, with white powder and rouge, sent flirtatious winks and giggles to the seated guests. Ah, money oppresses women, selling youth and soul. The increasing number of prostitutes in society is a prelude to the gradual decline of society.

On the music platform, a tune was played and another was changed. Revelers danced waltzes and blues, floral dances, tangos, as if the world had only this one night, and tomorrow people would part ways and drift into wandering journeys, filling with hedonism. Let us enjoy this short spring night to the fullest, let us be merry, people who have gathered temporarily on the journey! It made me hear a deep taste of sorrow, which I drank into my heart with bitter wine.

The night was deep, and amid the revelry and dancing of the lingering night, I had forgotten the passage of the night. I looked at my watch and it was already half past three in the morning. A bottle of beer had unknowingly been finished, so I left Venus among the revelry of men and women, burying my head in the collar of my spring coat. The spring breeze on the road was warm, and I still walked alone on the silent street to return to my residence, only the street lamp illuminated my shadow on the smooth asphalt road.

Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 160

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Finally, he tries to undo the knot, but is denied entry; Secretly pitying her innocence, he offers food to share

Thinking this, he immediately ran back to the house, sat on the kang (heated brick bed), and said with a stern face, "We are not from a lowly family, why do we let people look down on us like this?" Madam Jiang said, "Sigh! You don't need to mention this matter again. People have come to apologize to us, so that's enough. What else are you saying?" Guizhi originally wanted to tell her mother what she had just heard. But on second thought, her following Ji out was not a wise move, so she thought it best not to tell her mother. Therefore, she remained silent, lowered her head, and sat on the kang. The next morning, the Gan family's servant brought two dollars, saying that it was the payment for the clothes made before, and it was all settled now. According to the Second Master, the two dollars were only extra, and there would be no shortage. Guizhi heard this, and this was another sign of cutting off relations. She thought, she had never cared about the amount of wages when making clothes for the Second Master, and the Second Master saying such things meant that he also looked down on her. As she thought this in her heart, Madam Jiang had the same thought, and quickly ran outside the house and said, "We spend our strength to earn every penny. People as rich as your master and second master would certainly not let us poor people suffer, but we work properly with people and don't want extra money from them. I am a widow, and my child is a grown girl, why should we want extra money from people?" These words are not good to say or hear!" Madam Jiang said all this, and her face stiffened. The servant said, "Are you angry with me? These words were not said by me, nor by our Second Master. You are blaming the wrong person." After he finished speaking, he turned around and left. The arrival of this servant stirred up Guizhi's temper again, and she secretly resolved that she would not associate with the Gan family in the future, no matter what. From that day on, she did not go to the Gan family, but stayed at home with her mother to work. On the morning of the third day, because the water carrier had something to do and did not come, and the family was waiting for water to drink, Guizhi took a white iron bucket and carried a bucket of water from the well and walked towards the house. In the past, moving half a bucket of water at home did not feel strenuous, so she did not hesitate to carry a bucket of water back from the well. The distance from the well to the door was about half a mile, and she had to stop several times on the way before she had walked even a third of the way. (29)

Shanghai Night Talk: Smoking Shops 161

— Zhang Ruotun

Recently, in my spare time from work, I have added a new hobby of smoking cigarettes, in addition to sipping coffee.

I once made a vow: if I were to smoke, I would definitely smoke "Chesterfields." Because the large "Chesterfield" advertisements on the street, with their American modern romantic paintings, are especially captivating under the red and green electric lights. Moreover, the fragrant and beautiful lines, "When a girl is in the spring of her life, Chesterfields entice her," are so evocative!

Since I started learning to smoke, I have smoked many strange brands of cigarettes. My criteria for buying cigarettes is to choose brands with interesting names. My favorite on weekdays is "Charming Prince" (commonly known as "Taizi," or "Prince"), followed by "Black Cat." If I can't buy "Flowers of May," I buy domestic cigarettes "Xuangong" and "Tianxian." "Red Lips" are indeed very fragrant and alluring, but they are rarely popular on the market.

There is a cigarette shop near Zhenfei Road and Jin Shenfu Road that uses "Smoking Shop" as its name. It is a place I often visit. They display samples of various strange brands of cigarettes, all of which are rare on the market. There are almost ten kinds of Russian cigarettes alone, including "Caucasus" produced by Soviet Russia, and half-cigarettes with paper tubes made by White Russians; "Kismet," "Isis," "Ada," "Aliegro," etc.

At the intersection of Maierxi Ai Hongyi Main Road, opposite the Khitan Grand Theater, there is a Japanese-run grocery store that exclusively manages a French "National" brand of tricolor cigarettes. The fragrance is strong, with the aroma of cigars, and it does not dry the throat. After the September 18th Incident (Mukden Incident), I have not visited there for a long time.

The most exquisite cigarette cases include the silver hard iron box of "My Princess," and the "Monas," packaged in a paper box with twenty cigarettes. The most modern is the British-made "du Maurier," which comes in packs of ten or twenty. The cigarette tip is made of a hygienic wrinkled paper, like a cotton head, which is better than ordinary rubber tips. The price is very expensive, each cigarette costs twelve copper coins.

If someone likes to collect color movie star cards, I advise them to smoke the thick and fat "Commander" brand; if they like to collect colorful Western paintings, I advise them to smoke the "Tianxian" brand.

The original name of cigarette tobacco in English, as we all know, is called "Tobacco." The best Chinese translation is "Danbagu." In French it is "Tobaco," and in Spanish it is "Tabago."

The original discovery of tobacco is said to be in Tabasco, one of the British islands, and some say it is in Tobacco in the Gulf of Mexico. The name of tobacco is derived from these two place names.

Tobacco was first introduced to Europe by Spanish merchants, and became a daily pastime in France. The first to promote it was Jean Nicot, the ambassador to France appointed by Catherine de' Medici.

In addition to "Danbagu," there are many other meaningful nicknames for tobacco. As far as I know, there are "Danbugui" (don't return), "Nanmancao" (southern barbarian grass), "Nanlingcao" (southern spiritual grass), "Duobogu," "Xibagu," "Danpogu," "Xiangsicao" (love-sickness grass), etc.

Among modern literary works, the Japanese writer Yokomitsu Riichi's "The Lit Cigarette," also known as "The Misfortune of a Cigarette Collector," (contained in Guo Jianying's translation of Yokomitsu Riichi's collection "The Bridegroom's Thoughts") uses cigarettes as the subject matter.

Below is a short excerpt from that novel:

"I am now smoking cigarettes self-destructively, because I want to prove whether this thing is magic. Who would have thought that love would jump out of this hazy smoke? This is indeed a magic trick. Otherwise, it must be the harm of cigarettes. I now swear that I will never smoke again. ... Um, cigarettes are indeed harmful, let's light them and burn them. ... In his mind, countless lit cigarettes lined up, as if on a musical score, and began to swim towards him. | Dames-Opera-High Life-DaCapo-La Came-La Rubia..."

Free Talk

The Whole Line Outside the Pass is Peaceful and Safe 162

— Yang Xingzhi

Ever since Rehe fell "as expected," we had long anticipated that the "anti-Japanese comedy" had reached its "finale." Although the sounds of resistance are still incessant, and the telegrams requesting action are still generous and impassioned, some people are even shouting "unified military command" and "controlled economy," with the pretense of a "determination" to fight. But everyone already understands that this is just an "encore," a farcical pantomime. Sure enough, in the midst of the deafening cries of "saving the country with aviation," the entire line outside the pass seized the opportunity to quietly declare "peace and security."

What will happen after the whole line is peaceful? Based on the past experience of the September 18th and Shanghai battles, it will probably be nothing more than a "round table conference" or some kind of "agreement." However, things will still inevitably have some twists and turns. On the one hand, our "authorities" have repeatedly stated that the claim of "direct negotiations" is a "baseless rumor." On the other hand, according to the opinion of Japanese Ambassador to China Ariyoshi: "Now that Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, if China and Japan negotiate directly, it will invisibly raise China's international status." The tone also clearly has the meaning of "disdaining" to negotiate directly with us. If we do not "fight" and cannot "make peace," then how should the subsequent plays be staged? Of course, the most appropriate method is to "drag it out," drag it out for a year or so, and wait for "national understanding" (borrowing Ariyoshi's words) before making a decision.

The entire line outside the pass is already peaceful and safe. Although the northeast half of the country has changed color, it is indeed a gratifying thing that the Japanese can "know when to stop" and "not go too far." Moreover, according to Mr. ××: "The lost territory in the Northeast will definitely be recovered by the end of this year." So, there is no need to worry about this. But what we are most worried about right now is Ariyoshi's nonsense. He said: "Although the military leaders of the provinces have temporarily suspended the civil war due to external tension, the undercurrent is still surging, but they are all restrained by the criticism of the Chinese people and dare not become the leaders of the war themselves." Of course, under the declaration of "sincere unity and resistance to foreign aggression" by our military and political authorities over the past two years, we must not believe Ariyoshi's words to be true. However, "sincere unity" is for "resistance to foreign aggression." When there is no aggression to resist, who can guarantee that our generals will not feel that "the flesh on their thighs has grown back" and put on another comedy?

The "anti-Japanese" comedy is coming to an end, but audiences, please wait, the "best show" is yet to come!

Ferryman 163

— Qiu Peng

I first met him on an evening two years ago.

It was also this kind of early spring weather. Several friends and I passed by this ferry crossing. When we stepped into the ferry, the first person I saw was this ferryman. Such a withered old man, with sparse hair and beard, hunching his back, constantly coughing. Looking at his aged state, you wouldn't believe that he could row the oars so lightly and nimbly:

"Ferryman! Have you been eating this for a long time?"

"For a long time. Generations of family tradition, I've been doing this since I was a child."

"How is the daily income?"

"It's not bad. As long as I can ferry thirty times a day, five people each time, then each person pays two copper coins, which would be three thousand cash in profit, enough for the family to eat!"

A smile of contentment with life spread across his wrinkled face; while rowing the oars, he began to sing a mountain song: "In April, the wheat fields will meet with lovers..." He rocked us to the other side.

Afterward, I occasionally passed by this ferry crossing. The ferryman's optimistic smile and singing gradually left a cordial impression in my mind!

But last autumn, when I passed by the ferry crossing again, I suddenly saw that the usual happy look on his face had disappeared. I casually asked:

"Ferryman, why aren't you singing mountain songs?"

"How can I be in the mood to sing mountain songs: I can see that I'm about to have no food to eat!"

"What's the matter?"

"Tell you, sir: It's all because I, a poor man, talked too much! I recklessly offended a rich man and now I'm going to lose my life! A few days ago, the Third Master of ×× Garden passed by here. As soon as he got on the boat, he kept urging me to row faster and faster, wanting to row to the other side in one go. I didn't recognize him, and his urging made me angry, so I said: 'Sir, don't be too impatient! Ferries have to be rowed paddle by paddle like this; if you want to be fast, sir, you better build a bridge yourself!' Heavens! Just one sentence caused trouble! That Third Master immediately went back and hired workers to build a bridge. You know, rich people can do anything! Look, isn't there already someone here surveying for him? As soon as the bridge is built, our livelihood will be over!"

I followed his finger and saw several people building scaffolding and surveying on both banks!

"But why didn't you go and beg them for forgiveness in the first place?"

"Did you need to tell me that, sir! As soon as I got this news, my whole family immediately rushed to kneel in front of the Third Master, knocking our heads and begging for forgiveness. But what's the use? That person was already very angry. He said: 'Our Third Master has lived a lifetime and never suffered anyone's anger, but today I have to suffer the bird anger of you ferryman! I will definitely teach you this bastard to break your dog food bowl...' I'm old, and I can still manage to row and rest like this over such a short distance every day, but I can't handle changing careers and doing something else... You tell me, isn't my family's life over this time?"

The tragic voice made me not have the courage to turn around and look at his face. I hurriedly went ashore and left.

………………………………

The bridge was finally completed. The first time I stepped onto that magnificent stone bridge, I thought of the aged ferryman. I looked around, although I could no longer see the ferryman and his old ferry, but I seemed to see a pair of eyes filled with despair and resentment, staring unblinkingly at the passersby at the bridgehead.

Reducing Meals 164

— Jun Jian

"There is an urgent meeting after dinner, all students are expected to attend," our hero C reported in the dining hall.

Half past six in the afternoon.

Students came to the auditorium one after another. Our hero C, guarding the entrance of the auditorium, with a heroic aura, watched every student who came in. Finally, Miss Li arrived gracefully. Therefore, hero C jumped onto the stage and announced the start of the meeting.

The chairman was of course our hero C.

"The purpose of today's meeting is to reduce meals and use the food expenses we save to buy airplanes to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army!"

"The Easterners have invaded... the Volunteer Army is fighting the Japanese in the wind and dew... We college students, although we cannot take up guns and directly fight Japanese imperialism, must share the hardships with the Volunteer Army... reduce the food to the minimum..."

Our hero, lectured for half an hour, with great passion, especially when Miss Li applauded.

"Reduce meals by two dollars per person," our poet W proposed.

"One dollar!" Fat T proposed.

"..."

Passed: Reduce one dollar per person from the monthly food expenses of seven dollars.

Lunch on Saturday.

Athlete L, who is going out for a competition in the afternoon, needs to eat his fill.

One bowl, two bowls, the dishes are gone. Athlete L pouted, Xiao Wang at the same table also seemed dissatisfied, and Mr. Hu wrinkled his brows.

"Reducing meals is completely making fun of us poor boys, so they can show off!" Athlete L slammed the table.

Everyone was not full, and they were all indignant, and together they glared at our hero C.

On C's table were scrambled eggs, ribs, and pickled mustard greens stir-fried with shredded meat. Humph!

Athlete L's eyes turned red, he ran to the side and grabbed our hero C's new tie, which he had just changed today, and roared:

""We want to share the hardships with the Volunteer Army in the wind and dew," good, hero, let's go to the Northeast together, it's useless to just sing high praises in front of the misses, let's go!"

Poet W panicked and tried to dissuade him:

"Today is because we were afraid that guests would come, so we added these few dishes, it's not that we are eating well because everyone reduced meals."

Fat T also came to persuade:

"Why pull ties and resort to violence, we are all college students, don't act like savages."

This storm finally calmed down within half an hour.

Our hero C's tie was not broken, but it was a little crumpled, but it was still beautiful, so he didn't change to a new one, and hurriedly went to the Shanghai Grand Theater with poet W and fat T, because he was afraid that Miss Li would arrive first and be angry if she waited too long.

Not Allowed to Think 165

— E Jun

The first step in suppressing "reaction" is not allowing people to "move." The second step is not allowing people to "speak"; because speaking has the danger of inciting "movement," and if the "words" are written on paper, the danger is even greater. But the problem with speaking is that the brain will "think": so, in order to thoroughly suppress "reaction," it is necessary to not allow people to "think."

Now, the first step in suppressing "reaction" seems to have been successful. The second step is probably not far from success either. It's just that implementing the third step is a bit difficult. But we must not think that we will never think of it.

Today is the era of all-powerful science. Radio can send the speeches of important people to the ears of young masters and misses, and the shadow of the late detective novelist Conan Doyle can appear in photographs (see reports from last year). In the future, there may be a "Royal Scientist" who wins the Nobel Prize, racking his brains to invent a machine or a mirror that can capture the shadows of hundreds of millions of people and the secret thoughts hidden in their hearts, magnify them with a magnifying glass, and present them to the gentlemen who "uphold the Way." At that time, all demons and monsters will have nowhere to escape, and even those who appear upright but harbor evil intentions will be caught one by one and punished with the crime of "having bad intentions." In this way, everyone will naturally become good people obediently, not moving, not speaking, and also not daring to think. At that time, the country will be in order, the hunting dogs will be useless, and the gentlemen who "uphold the Way" will have no "Way" to "uphold," and they can just sit and hug beautiful women, leisurely and carefree, to pass the long days.

The Crossroads of the Times and Love 166

— Zhang Guiping

"Li Yixiang is out of his mind, pay him no attention..."

Haiquan knew that Tang Yaoxing was a disciple of Chen Huamin and seemed to have little faith in Li Yixiang. But Haiquan liked Li Yixiang's new poems, so he felt a slight antipathy towards Tang Yaoxing.

"Constructivist art is probably mechanist art."

Haiquan had once briefly skimmed a book on the theory of mechanist literature and art, so he brought it up to Yaoxing.

"Writing Wu Zetian as a revolutionary sister, supported by the masses. Is that considered Constructivist art?"

Haiquan saw that Yaoxing's attitude was so arrogant, and his question was irrelevant to the answer, so he was really unconvinced. But there was nothing he could do, so he kept quiet.

Everyone ate refreshments and chatted aimlessly for a while. Seeing that it was getting late, Chen Huamin stood up again.

"If you all have no suggestions or questions, then let's adjourn the meeting. However, before adjourning, I have a brief report. Starting next week, the S Society headquarters has decided to send Propaganda Minister Mr. Cheng to guide us in studying revolutionary theory. Once a week. However, the time and place cannot be predetermined. We will notify you temporarily at that time. This is the most important task. Please be sure to participate enthusiastically. That's all."

Haiquan hesitated a little after hearing this. He had originally joined this literary group to study literature and art, but he had not expected that this literary group would also entail many tasks, such as demonstrations, revolutionary issues, social problem studies, etc. He thought, even if there is no danger, it's too much trouble. But only for a moment, he reproached himself.

"Stand on the front line, don't be so unambitious in your thinking!"

He secretly encouraged himself and then bid farewell to them. When he walked to Li Yixiang, whom he had always admired, to say goodbye, Yixiang hurriedly pulled a pair of palms from his sleeves and tightly grasped his hand. Haiquan felt that Yixiang's hand had a warm and smooth feeling similar to that of a woman.

"Wait a moment, let's walk together. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . ."

Haiquan was truly flattered to be retained by this great writer, and he was indescribably happy. He hurriedly stood aside, watching Li Yixiang and another tall man whispering to each other. He also talked to those young people one by one, all using this set of formulas, first whispering for a while, then shaking hands, and finally laughing loudly, repeatedly saying, "I have a way, I have a way!"

Haiquan saw that Chen Huamin's attitude seemed to disapprove of Li Yixiang's actions, frowning and smiling bitterly with his thick lips, but he dared not say anything.

Choosing a Radio (3) 186

— Xiong

Choosing a radio requires examining your own needs. Now, let's analyze everyone's needs first:

(1) Amateur Research. Since it is research in nature, you can choose any radio, from crystal sets to the latest and most complex long and shortwave radios, without any problem.

(2) For Individual Use. This refers to listening with headphones only. Near the broadcast station, you can purchase a crystal set, but it is also limited to places where there are not too many broadcast stations and the radio waves do not interfere. It is not possible in Shanghai. A single-tube regenerative receiver can be used farther away from the broadcast station. For even greater distances, add high-frequency amplification. If you want louder sound, you need to add low-frequency amplification.

(3) For Family Use. This does not require excessive loudness, as it will disturb neighbors and cause resentment. It is enough for the whole family to be able to hear. You can add two stages of low-frequency amplification to the level that can be heard individually, or use the new pentode tube for amplification.

(4) For Public Use. This requires a rich volume of sound, so it is convenient to purchase a ready-made radio.

(5) For Travel Use, or Mobile Use. Because you cannot install a ground and antenna, you must choose a good radio.

Secondly, the power supply must also be given considerable consideration. Crystal sets do not require a power supply, so it is unnecessary to say, all vacuum tube radios must have a power supply. In remote mountain villages where there is no electric lighting, it is necessary to use dry batteries for everything. In some places, there is electricity at night but no electricity during the day, so storage batteries can be used to supply A power. If there is electricity day and night, you can use an AC radio.

The electricity from electric lighting factories in various places is either direct current or alternating current. You cannot use an AC machine with direct current, and you cannot use a DC machine with alternating current. Even with alternating current, the voltage is different, some use 110 volts and some use 220 volts. Therefore, before purchasing, you must consider it carefully.

There are many types of radios sold on the market today, and lecturers often struggle to choose. But these radios each have their own unique points, such as being cheap, sounding good, being easy to carry, or having authentic sound. We cannot strongly point out which is superior and which is inferior. However, if you can purchase according to the local situation and your own needs, it will be both economical and convenient. In the future, when I have time, I plan to give a brief analysis of the characteristics of various radios on the market and which ones are suitable for which situations.

Principles and Transmission of Micro-Wave Radio 187

— Shi Huayu

A few months ago, this newspaper had a piece of news saying that the International Telegraph Company successfully tested micro-wave radio telephone from London to Paris. It also said that the antenna of this shortwave transmitter is less than one inch long, and the number of vibrations per second can reach 300 million times.

This type of shortwave is O Quasi Optical Sboitwave, and all wavelengths from 10 meters to several centimeters belong to it. Therefore, its wavelength is close to the wavelength of light waves. The generation of this shortwave uses vacuum tubes. However, its wave generation method is different from ordinary ones, because it uses Electron Oscilfation. What is electron oscillation, please see Figure 1:

Figure 1: Filament F passes current and generates electrons due to heat, but the grid G surrounds F and is charged with high-voltage positive electricity, so the electrons generated by F are attracted by G. At the same time, because the area of ​​G is extremely small, most of the electrons are not absorbed by it but pass through the grid holes and proceed to the screen P which is charged with a higher negative voltage. But at a certain point Figure 2

, due to the repulsion of the same polarity, the electrons are rejected and returned. The dotted line in the figure indicates the path of electron travel. Because the number of cycles of electrons being attracted and repelled per second is extremely high, it is used as electron oscillation. The simplest electron. The simplest electron oscillation circuit is shown in Figure 2.

Figure 3: Receiver Antenna Line Transmitter Antenna Line

V is 99 or 27. All vacuum tubes with cylindrical screens are applicable.

AA is a copper tube used to install the antenna.

Figure 3 shows the installation of a radiating and receiving antenna:

Other things such as wavelength meters and receiving circuits cannot be described in detail due to space limitations, and will be described in another article when I have time.

Figures in the Radio World: Ohm 188

— KP

丨The discoverer of Ohm's law丨

Ohm (Geory Simon Ohm 1787-1854) was a German physicist, born in Erlungon on the upper reaches of the Main River in southern Germany. In 1817, he served as a professor at the Jesuit University of Cologne. In 1833, he became a professor at the Nuremberg Higher Industrial School. In 1852, he became a professor of experimental physics at the University of Munich, and later died in Menz. His writings are mostly about the theory of current, especially Galvani sche Kette Mathematisch Bearbeitet, published in Berlin in 1827, which is the most famous. Ohm's law, which shows the relationship between current, voltage, and resistance, was discovered by him. Therefore, the unit of resistance is called "Ohm" to commemorate his contribution. Ohm's theory of current is very similar to Faraday's theory of heat conduction. If we use temperature in Faraday's theory as potential and current as sound flow, then it can be said that it is completely the same as Ohm's theory.

Inspection and Handling of Radio Obstacles AA 189

(2) Low Sound

The sound of the radio gradually becoming low is a common problem and also the most annoying problem. If this problem is not cured, how disappointing is it?

Now I will tell you the inspection method and handling method for this problem:

Phenomenon Reason Handling Method

The sound naturally gradually decreases Vacuum tube aging Apply the "revival method" or replace with a new one

Crystal is insensitive Replace with a good one or explore other contacts

High consumption resistor is defective Replace with a good one

Battery voltage decreases Charge

The resistance at the connection is too high File the overweight connection

The ground and antenna are defective Pay attention to inspection and repair

The sound is sometimes high and sometimes low The voltage of the electric light wire supplying B power changes (AC) For those with tap terminals on the power transformer, replace them.

The sound does not change at all when the antenna is removed The antenna connection is poor or there is a break in the lead-in wire or the ground wire connection is poor Pay attention to inspection and repair

Experience 190

— Li Yuanqing

A Once-and-for-All Improvement to Single-Wire Antennas

Ordinary lead-in wires are probably wrapped around or soldered on the antenna. After a long time, they are prone to loosening. If a small part is left on the length of the antenna itself as the lead-in wire (see figure), then it will not change no matter how long it takes. Moreover, reducing the length of the antenna can also increase selectivity, which is especially needed in Shanghai, where there are many broadcast stations.

Wind-Resistant Movable Pull Wire

If the antenna pull wire is too tight, it is easy to be blown off by the wind. If it is too loose, the efficiency will be reduced and the appearance will not be good. It is best to pass the pull wire through a pulley and hang an iron hammer of appropriate weight below. In this way, the iron hammer can automatically adjust the tightness of the antenna.

A Burnt Vacuum Tube Transforms into a Vacuum Tube's Lifesaver

Soak the burnt-out or old and useless vacuum tube in boiling water. After a few minutes, the glass tube can be detached. The remaining rubber tube can be used to install a small electric bulb of considerable voltage (see figure). During testing, insert the rubber tube into the lamp holder before inserting the vacuum tube to measure whether the filament voltage is misconnected. This can avoid many unexpected losses.

Small Light Bulb Filament Foot Lamp Wire Socket Fire

All Kinds of Antennas (Continued) 191

— Jin Yunqiao

(2) Multi-Wire Type: Or when the environment is not suitable for installing a single-wire type, a multi-wire type can be used. Two or three wires of equal length can be installed in parallel according to the single-wire method. The length of each wire should not be shorter than 10 meters, and the distance between each wire must be more than one foot. The capacitance of this type is larger than that of a single wire.

(3) V-Shaped Type: It is excellent for places where the location is cramped. This type has two directions in one wire, and the number of radio stations that can be received is more than that of a single direction. The lead-in wire is best connected to the corner of the V-shape.

(4) Cage Type: According to actual experiments, the resistance of this type is smaller than that of the flat-top type, and the efficiency is better. However, it is troublesome to install and few people use it. The height is about 20 meters and the length of each wire is about 25 meters.

(5) Umbrella Type: This type is mostly used in large radio stations to enhance the scattering ability of radio waves.

(6) Filter Type: This type is based on the transformer principle.

,(as shown in Figure 2) 1 is the center wire, which can be made of 18-gauge fabric-covered wire. Its function is similar to the primary coil of a transformer. Both ends are grounded to form a large loop. 2 is a finer enameled wire of 300 feet, surrounding the outside of the center wire, just like the secondary coil of a transformer. The electric wave is induced into the center wire and then induced into the outer antenna coil, plus the second Figure: Lead-In Wire Ground

the voltage of the electric wave induced by the antenna coil itself, so the received sound is stronger than that of an ordinary antenna.

In addition to the above-mentioned types of outdoor antennas, there are also L-shaped, fan-shaped, loop-shaped, T-shaped, and other types, all of which are named differently due to their different forms. Due to space limitations, I will not list them one by one. The overhead wires of electric lights can also be used as antennas (as shown in Figure 3). 1 is any wire of the electric light, which is used as an antenna (two wires can also be used together, but two fixed storage capacitors must be installed, or one wire can be used as an antenna and one wire can be used as a ground wire, both are acceptable). 2 is a switch or a knife switch, 3 is a fixed capacitor, and its capacity is about 0002MF.D. It must be able to withstand Figure 3: Ground Wire

high voltage, otherwise there is a risk of burning out. However, it is best not to use electric light wires as antennas because there are many dangers.

(B) Indoor Antenna (1) Loop Type: This type uses a cross-shaped wooden frame (or metal frame) and wraps several turns of insulated copper wire to form a square or rectangle, or other geometric shapes are also possible (as shown in Figure 4). The length of an ordinary parallel antenna is longer than that of a loop type, so the capacitance is larger, but the inductance is smaller. It must be equipped with a relatively large induction coil. Because the loop antenna is wound into a loop, although the inductance is larger, its sound reception ability is far inferior to that of an outdoor antenna.

A loop antenna is just an enlarged version of a coil. The distance between each turn is proportional to the inductance. The closer the distance, the greater the inductance and the fewer the number of turns should be; the farther the distance, the smaller the inductance and the more the number of turns should be. For ordinary loop antennas that receive 200 to 500 meters of electricity, if the length of the wooden frame from A to B and from C to B (see Figure 4) is 20 inches, and the distance between each post is 10 inches, 16 turns is enough. If the distance is a quarter of an inch, 14 turns can also be used.

Wireless Radio Knowledge (5) 192

— Wei

(5) Ohm's Law

As mentioned above, there are some conductors through which electricity flows easily, and there are some through which it does not flow easily. This is because conductors have different resistance to current. Metals are generally good conductors of electricity, so they are also called good conductors. On the other hand, there are many substances through which electricity can barely flow, but the resistance is very high, which easily weakens the current. These are called poor conductors. As for many substances such as glass, porcelain, and oil, their electrical resistance is so high that current cannot pass through them, so they are called insulators. Various machines are actually ingenious combinations of good conductors, poor conductors, and insulators.

Then, what is the relationship between current, voltage, and resistance?

If the water pressure is high, the water flow is large, and the resistance is large (for example, using a thin pipe to pass water)

It can be said that it is directly proportional to the water pressure and inversely proportional to the resistance. Current

, and inversely proportional to the resistance. If we use a formula to express it, it is as follows

Current (Amperes) = Voltage (Volts) / Resistance (Ohms)

Ampere is the unit of current, Volt is the unit of voltage, and Ohm is the unit of resistance (please refer to the article "Units of Electricity" published in this publication). It is common to use I to represent current, E to represent voltage, and R to represent resistance. So the above formula becomes

I = E / R

This formula was discovered by the German Ohm (please refer to the "Figures in the Radio World" in this issue), so it is also called Ohm's Law. This law is a very important basic principle for us to study electricity and radio. It is applicable to both alternating current and direct current. From this law, we can design various machines (of course, there are also more complicated formulas). It means that if a voltage of E volts is applied to a conductor with a resistance of R ohms, a current of one ampere can be obtained. If the voltage is doubled, the current will also be doubled. If the resistance is doubled, the current will be halved. If we change the above formula into an algebraic formula, then (1)

E = IR

This means that in order to pass a current of I amperes through a conductor with a resistance of R ohms, a voltage of E volts must be applied. Also (2)

R = E / I

This means that if a voltage of E is applied to both ends of a conductor and the current flowing through it is I amperes, then the resistance of the conductor is R ohms. Using this formula, we can calculate the ohm value of the filament resistor (Rbeostat) of a vacuum tube radio. For example, the UX20IA vacuum tube only requires a filament voltage of 5 volts and a current of 25 amperes. If a 6-volt storage battery is used, the voltage is one volt higher and a resistor must be used to reduce it. So

R = E / I = (6-5) / 0.25 = 1 / 0.25 = 4 Ohms

This means that the resistor must be at least 4 ohms. If a 6-ohm bleeder resistor is used, it is very safe.

Page 20

If the wooden frame is reduced to 16 inches on each side, with each turn a quarter of an inch apart, there are 16 turns. If they are half an inch apart, there are 20 turns. With a 0.0005 M.F.D. variable capacitor, its center Ding to Wu should be at least 8 inches apart. Although a loop antenna with a smaller area is easy to carry, its effectiveness is inferior.

A loop antenna has directivity. When its plane is opposite to the power station, the received electric wave is the strongest, and when it is at right angles, it is the weakest. The direction finder used on ships is also made according to this principle. There is also a complex loop antenna, which has a small loop inside a large loop, and is used in special circuits (to be continued).

Units of Electricity (3) 193

— Jun

(4) Unit of Resistance

The strength of an electric current is related not only to the magnitude of electromotive force but also to the type and shape of the conductor. The current generated from the same battery (i.e., equal electromotive force) will be stronger if a copper wire is used as the conductor than if an iron wire is used. If the same type of conductor is used, the current will be stronger if the shape is shorter and thicker than if it is longer and thinner. This property of the conductor, which impedes the current and reduces its strength, is called Resistance, or impediment. Each conductor has a certain resistance. The unit of resistance is called the Ohm, or simply Ohm. One Ohm is the resistance presented when the voltage across a conductor is one volt and the current intensity is one ampere. In practice, it is equal to the resistance presented by a mercury column at zero degrees Celsius with a cross-section of one square millimeter and a length of 106.3 centimeters to an unvarying current.

Resistance is represented by the letter R in formulas.

Two other units are used to measure larger or smaller resistances:

Megohm (symbol MU): one million ohms

Micromho (symbol MU): one millionth of an ohm

(1) One UX tube socket, one RCA232 or other equivalent brand vacuum tube

(2) One UY tube socket, one RCA233 or other pentode vacuum tube

If you want to listen with headphones, the plate current is too large and the coil can easily burn out. The C-battery should be changed to 22.5 volts, or the B-battery should be changed to 90 volts before it can be used.

Also, it should be noted that the top electrode of the tetrode vacuum tube used as a detector is the grid, and one of the tube feet corresponding to the usual triode grid position is the screen grid, which should be connected to 22.5 volts of B-battery. Features of the Stewart 106 Radio (Continued) 196

— Zhenzhi

○ Squelch Circuit

○The connection between the squelch circuit and the suppression of noise between stations is as follows. If a radio has only an inter-station noise suppressor, it will not completely eliminate the high-pitched strikes of static electricity. If the sensitivity of the radio is reduced to the point where it can completely eliminate static electricity strikes, the result will inevitably be that the radio waves of all the powerful stations in this city will also be completely expelled.

The function of the squelch circuit is to limit the radio to receiving only sound signals above a certain predetermined intensity, and to isolate all sound signals or static noise below this intensity. The curve in Figure 2 shows the volume of a sound signal on an ordinary radio as it gradually tunes in to the point where it gradually tunes out. This line rises from point A, where there is no sound at all, to point B, where it is loudest, and gradually decreases to point C, where there is no sound at all. If the radio uses a Q-circuit, a completely different result can be obtained when it tunes into a certain station again. At this time, the sound received appears suddenly at point D. There is no hissing noise before the sound appears. If we continue to tune, we can hear this sound signal proceeding along the DBE curve. When it reaches point P, the Q-circuit immediately shows its function again, suddenly cutting off the weak hissing sound below it.

From this, it can be seen that another feature of the Q-circuit is that it can obviously improve the selectivity of the radio, because the sound signal from the station now tunes in only to the FG section, unlike an ordinary radio, which must be the entire AC section. If the Q-circuit is used in conjunction with the inter-station noise suppressor, it is not necessary to excessively weaken the sharpness when tuning between two stations, because the cut-off effect of the Q-circuit will effectively prevent the intrusion of static noise and various noises.

Here we must note that because of the existence of this Q-circuit, a new obstacle may occasionally occur, but this is easily eliminated. Suppose there is a very weak station at one point controlled by the inter-station noise suppressor, and its highest sound signal cannot exceed the length of the DF line in Figure 2, then the Q-circuit will receive the high-pitched part of this sound signal and cut off its weaker sounds, making the sound signal received a suffocating sound. The method of preventing this is very simple, just slightly increase the power of the inter-station noise suppressor, and then the sound signal will be clear and without obstacles.

Delayed Automatic Volume Control

In the past, in ordinary radios, when they received broadcasts from any station, whether the station was strong or weak, the automatic volume control function would immediately exert its function. This device could weaken the power of the low station sound signal to the point where it could not be heard.

The feature of the 106 model is that it can prevent the automatic volume control from working on the sound signals of weaker stations, because it is not necessary. However, if a station is encountered whose volume is extremely large and sufficient to supply full output, this automatic volume control will immediately show its effect. Even if ordinary radios have extremely convenient automatic volume control, there is often a fading phenomenon when receiving sound signals from weaker stations. This delayed automatic volume control can reduce this drawback. (The End)

The trains stopped at the Xuzhou station overnight and were scheduled to leave for Nanjing at 4:30 a.m. on the 1st, arriving in Shanghai that evening for shipment. According to the escorting officials, most of the Palace Museum's treasures have been transported, leaving only crude and bulky antique items. Whether to make a fourth shipment south will be decided by the Executive Yuan. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 31st)

Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai This Morning to Discuss the Central Government's Early Promulgation of the Constitution 220

Abolish the Provisional Constitution and the Guidelines for Political Tutelage, Return Political Power to the People

The Government's Foreign Policy Remains Unchanged, Hoping for Unity to Resist Aggression

Xin Sheng She reported that Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, along with legislators Ma Chaojun and Fu Bingchang, left Beijing by train at around 11 p.m. last night and arrived in Shanghai at 8 a.m. this morning. Xin Sheng She reporters visited Mr. Sun at his private residence on Columbia Road this morning. Mr. Sun stated that the Central Government has decided to convene the National Assembly early, promulgate the Constitution early, open up political power, and return it to the people. Mr. Sun also stated that the Central Government's foreign policy remains unchanged and hopes that the whole country will unite and mobilize to resist Japan and defend against foreign aggression. A detailed record of Mr. Sun's remarks is as follows:

(Opening Up Political Power) (Reporter asked) Does the Central Government's decision to open up political power mean abandoning one-party rule, or does it mean returning the power held by a few to the majority? (Mr. Sun said) The Third Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Executive Committee resolved to convene the National Assembly in April of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Now, it has been decided to hold it earlier and promulgate the Constitution early. However, this issue still needs to be decided by the National Congress in July of this year. There is no such thing as opening up political power, because the Constitution has already been promulgated early, and the Provisional Constitution and the Guidelines for Political Tutelage established by the Central Political Council during the period of political tutelage have become obsolete. The government has returned political power to the people. Since political power is jointly owned by the people, there is no such thing as opening it up. (Asked) Will one-party rule be abandoned at that time? Should the Constitution explicitly stipulate that the people are allowed to freely establish political parties? (Answered) Since the Constitution has been promulgated and the people have freedom of assembly and association, then the establishment of political parties is also permitted by the Constitution. There is naturally no need for explicit provisions in the Constitution.

(Participation in Politics) He also said that the organization of the National Political Council is currently under review by the Legislative Yuan. Now that the National Congress has been brought forward to July, deciding on the issue of convening a provisional National Assembly, the National Political Council is no longer necessary to convene, because the National Assembly is the highest organ of the government, and the National Political Council is only a popular opinion organ during the transitional period. If the National Assembly is convened early, the Constitution must of course be promulgated early, and its drafting period must also be shortened. As for the organizational law and election law of the National Assembly, the principles can be roughly decided by the Central Political Council next week.

(Unity to Resist Aggression) The government has no diplomacy to speak of with Japan. Ambassador Jiang has also been recalled. From now on, diplomacy will only be possible if we can resist Japan. This consistent policy has not changed. Currently, the Central Government's anti-Japanese military efforts are focused on consolidating positions. If we attack, we can recover lost territory. If we defend, we can maintain existing territory. Otherwise, we will not even be able to defend, let alone attack. Therefore, unity is a prerequisite for national mobilization. To achieve this goal, we must also reform politics and increase strength. What we regret most now is that China is not a purely unified country. Government orders cannot reach the borders, local autonomy in the provinces has not been completed, and there is a gap between public opinion and the government. Therefore, the majority opinion advocates: (1) Concentrating and uniting national public opinion, convening the National Assembly early, promulgating the Constitution early, and opening up political power. (2) Reforming politics so that the central government and the provinces can work together effectively and strictly adhere to discipline. (3) Implementing local autonomy and communicating public opinion. Only when these three things are accomplished can we have the strength to resist Japan. Otherwise, everything will be empty talk and of no practical use.

(Hoping for Feng Yuxiang to Go South) Mr. Sun finally said that the Central Government has hoped that Feng Yuxiang would go south since last year. There have been exchanges of letters and telegrams, and people have been sent to Zhangjiakou to urge him. I estimate that Feng should be able to take on considerable responsibility, but the title has not yet been determined.

Water Supply in Beijing City Has Been Restored 221

(Nanjing) The water supply in Beijing City has been restored from Gulou southwards starting on the 1st. (Special dispatch on the 1st)

Deteriorating Situation of Anti-Semitism in Germany 222

The Propaganda Department Issues a Notice of Temporary Boycott. The Paris International League Also Boycotts German Goods

▲Reuters, Berlin, March 31. Dr. Goebbels, Minister of Propaganda, announced on the radio tonight that the National Socialist Party's movement to boycott Jews nationwide, which began at 10 a.m. on Saturday, will end that evening. However, if the "cruel propaganda" made by overseas Jews does not completely cease, the boycott movement will resume on April 5. According to Goebbels, the "cruel propaganda" of overseas Jews has greatly declined recently, indicating that the National Socialist Party's boycott intimidation has been effective. He also claimed that German Jews have the absolute power to restrict or stop "cruel propaganda." Goebbels concluded by saying that if it is necessary to resume the boycott on April 5, the way it is implemented will be enough to destroy the Jewish people throughout Germany. "However, we want to get along with the world. We want to work and do not want to make enemies for no reason." The National Socialist Party's stormtroopers are actively carrying out the anti-Semitic movement. Although today is not yet the day of implementation, they have already begun to act, excluding all Jewish judges and lawyers from the Berlin courts. Shortly after, the National Socialist Party headquarters ordered non-Jewish employees of Jewish businesses to pre-pay two months' salary and to demonstrate against their Jewish owners outside their stores at 3 p.m. on Saturday. At the same time, non-Jewish store owners were ordered to immediately dismiss their Jewish employees, but Jewish owners were not allowed to dismiss their non-Jewish employees. The National Socialist Party headquarters is now appointing commissioners to punish Jewish owners who disobey. The National Socialist Party is also imitating the methods of the Middle Ages, ordering all Jewish shops to hang large black and yellow signs outside. The police chief of Altona even ordered the words "Jewish Business" to be added to the sign. Various slogans are now posted throughout the country, such as "International Jews must now admit that they cannot turn Germany into a colony of Soviet Russian criminals," and denying the various acts of anti-Semitism, also stating "Overseas Jews are at war with the German people," blaming the Jews in Germany. Schleicher published a radical article in the newspaper, saying "Since the Jews started this war, this war must continue until the Jews admit that the Germany governed by the Brownshirts is not comparable to the Germany governed by cowards." The passports of important Jewish figures have now been cancelled to prevent them from leaving the country.

▲Reuters, Berlin, March 31. The boycott of Jews will end on Saturday night. Outsiders see this as the Germans having recognized that a long-term boycott will inevitably lead to economic chaos. The cessation of the boycott must be due to the advocacy of the National Socialist Party members in the cabinet. Many people believe that this anti-Semitic movement is not entirely a self-defense action in retaliation for the "cruel propaganda" made by overseas Jews. The main reason is that the extreme elements of the National Socialist Party have been advocating anti-Semitism for many years and have never had a chance to do so. Therefore, the leaders of the National Socialist Party intend to use this action to vent their anger. Whether this appeasement policy will be effective is still in question. All sectors of the Jewish community are deeply concerned that once the boycott movement begins, it will be out of control. Although the leaders of the National Socialist Party want it to end that evening, they fear that they will not be able to restrain the party members in time. Therefore, Goebbels' speech did not alleviate this panic.

▲Havas, Berlin, March 31. Deputy Minister of Finance, a Jew named Seton, resigned today. There are now no traces of Jews in the public service of the federal government and the Prussian ministries.

▲Havas, Berlin, March 31. Stormtroopers of the National Socialist Party occupied the Court of Appeals in Königsberg, prohibiting Jews from entering. Only a few Jewish lawyers are allowed to settle lawsuits for their co-religionists, but only if those lawyers can prove that they fought on the front lines during the European War.

▲Reuters, Paris, March 31. The International League has decided today to begin boycotting German goods as a retaliatory measure against the German Socialist Party's anti-Semitic movement. The League's boycott of German goods will begin tomorrow at the same time as the Socialist Party's anti-Semitic movement. All those who have ordered goods from German merchants have cancelled their orders. At the same time, a committee to protect abused Jews has been organized, and many leaflets and slogans are being printed.

(Havas, Astende, Belgium, March 31) The great German scientist Professor Einstein and his family are temporarily residing nearby. Einstein sent a letter to the Belgian news agency, stating that he did indeed send a letter to the German ambassador to Belgium on Thursday, informing him of his renunciation of German citizenship.

British Finances Are Sound 224

▲Reuters, London, March 31. The British annual revenue and expenditure statistics were released today, showing the sound position of the British budget. Revenue totaled £744,791,000, while expenditure, including the £17,250,000 allocated for debt repayment reserve, totaled £748,124,000, a shortfall of £3,323,000. In addition, the £28,956,000 paid to the US in December for war debts brought the total deficit to £32,279,000. Since last July, Britain could have received £30,250,000 in Allied war debts and reparations owed to Britain, calculated at the current exchange rate, and another £7,250,000 in war debts from overseas autonomous territories, totaling £37,500,000, to offset the debts owed to the US. However, according to the Lausanne Agreement, reparations and war debts are temporarily suspended until the Lausanne Agreement is ratified or a decision is made not to ratify it, resulting in Britain's expenditure exceeding its revenue. If all debts owed to Britain since last July had been paid as usual, the British budget would have had a surplus of £5,250,000. The budget did not include revenue and expenditure items such as reparations and war debts, only projecting total revenue of £766,800,000 and total expenditure of £766,000,000, which included a debt repayment reserve of £32,500,000. In terms of actual revenue, income tax and surtax collected £312,200,000 last year, £13,750,000 less than budgeted. Property tax collected £66,000,000, £1,000,000 more than budgeted. Customs duties and excise tax collected £288,000,000, £12,000,000 less than budgeted. Various loans exceeded the budget by £6,250,000. On the expenditure side, the original plan was to pay £276,000,000 for debt principal and interest, and £32,500,000 for the debt repayment reserve. As for the repayment of US debt, it is found in the Ministry of Finance's report as another item in the annual financial statement, indicating its special nature. The British government is entitled to consider the payment of this sum as a repayment of capital, which should be regarded as part of the final repayment in the future. Last year, in addition to paying US war debts, Britain actually paid £262,250,000 for debt principal and interest, and another £17,250,000 for the debt repayment reserve. In addition, £2,655,000 was paid for interest on savings bonds, which were repaid with loans. The allocation of the debt repayment reserve was lower than the amount projected in the budget, which was due to the impact of the high market price of national bonds after the wartime bonds were exchanged. The Ministry of Finance previously allowed the Bank of England to continue issuing £15,000,000 in banknotes without cash collateral. This right to issue banknotes will expire tonight, and the Bank of England has not requested to continue to enjoy this right. Therefore, the issuance of this credit currency will be reduced from £275,000,000 to £260,000,000 to match the total amount of legal tender when Britain suspended the gold standard in September 1931.

Poland Opposes the Four-Power Pact. This Draft Violates the League of Nations Covenant. 225

▲Havas, London, March 31. It is generally known that Polish Foreign Minister Beck recently told the British Ambassador to Poland that the Polish government had not received formal notification of the Anglo-Italian talks, so it seemed that no comment should be made on the draft Four-Power Treaty. However, the Polish government believes that this draft is contrary to both the letter and spirit of the League of Nations Covenant, and therefore declares in advance that any resolutions adopted by a group of great powers organized on the basis of Italian proposals cannot bind Poland.

The Expanding American Banking Panic 226

(Second Letter) (March 1)

The Michigan Banking Crisis Creates a New Banking Panic. All government and Federal Reserve Bank countermeasures to quell the banking panic have been ineffective. The panic is spreading like wildfire and is expanding daily. Michigan, Ohio, Indiana, Illinois, Maryland, New Jersey, Iowa, Oklahoma, Wisconsin, Nebraska, Florida, Arkansas, Missouri, and California have all been engulfed in the vortex of the panic. Fourteen of the forty-eight states in the United States are now in a state of panic. More importantly, the panic has directly approached New York and is directly threatening Wall Street, the fortress of the gold kings.

On February 25, the government of Maryland announced that all 205 banks (with a total capital of 88.9 million gold dollars) would be allowed to restrict withdrawals, because the total amount of money withdrawn in the state in the past week, only 13 million gold dollars, was a very small number and had shaken the Baltimore banks. This is a signal indicating the extreme weakening of the banking situation, a signal indicating how dangerous this situation is, a signal indicating why hundreds of banks were forced to close due to small initial disturbances.

On February 27, the banking panic continued to expand. All deposits in Cleveland (Ohio) and Indianapolis were only allowed to withdraw 5 percent. All savings deposits were suspended for 30 days. Five banks in Akron (Ohio) with a total of 65 million gold dollars in deposits and 100 million gold dollars in capital were only allowed to withdraw 1 percent of deposits per month. Banks in Lima (Ohio) implemented restrictions on payments. Banks in Arkansas, Wisconsin, and Missouri were also forced to close.

Great efforts were made to rescue the 500 banks in Michigan that were in a state of panic. Ford (Henry Ford) was not forced to rescue his private banks until he was under the greatest pressure. He had been watching for a long time. His main reason was that, in his view, the entire banking system in the United States was bound to collapse. But in the end, he decided to reorganize the capital of his private banks and increase it to 8.25 million gold dollars. However, this number was relatively small, because the "Finance Reorganization Association" (RFC), a national rescue agency, had paid out 78 million gold dollars, the Federal Reserve Bank had paid out 20 million gold dollars, and the Chicago Bank had paid out 20 million gold dollars to cope with the payment of 30 percent of the deposits.

At the same time, the Washington government, with lightning speed, promulgated a decree giving the "Monetary Standard Supervisor" the power to prohibit the withdrawal of deposits from national banks. All 6,150 banks that complied with the Federal Reserve Bank's regulations were included in the list of those not allowed to withdraw deposits. But whether this bank commissioner with such great power can be effective if he does not have new and greater sums of money for rescue is still a big question.

It is now very clear that all the work of the Finance Reorganization Association in rescuing banks has not been successful. As early as January, 348 banks had already experienced panic. The number of banks forced to close and restrict payments in February must be over 1,000. The Finance Reorganization Committee carried out rescue work last year and is also engaged in this work now, but the current rescue work requires the state to give it tens of millions of dollars. However, if the state pays such a large sum of money at this time, it cannot but cause a serious danger to the monetary standard.

In this way, the banking panic once again raises the issue of the monetary standard sharply. The new generation of people centered on Roosevelt seem to want to maintain the gold standard. But all their explanations are not enough to prevent the depreciation of the gold dollar. If the banking panic continues to expand and new assistance is needed, it is still a question whether the government will not be forced to change its view of the monetary standard. For the time being, the government is still supporting the monetary standard without assisting the banks.

However, it is not impossible for the monetary standard to become unsustainable with the continued sharpening of the banking panic.

Although economists continue to try to obscure the international significance of this new panic, they cannot but admit that this American banking panic is a new start to the capitalist world panic, and is a start on a higher basis. Now we only need to study the shocks that the American banking panic has already caused and will inevitably cause in the entire international credit transactions to know its international significance.

On February 26, the Berliner Tageblatt expressed its support for Pinrell, saying that the dream of "the end of the panic" has now been awakened. "The galaxy in the world economy, which had previously given important light to the Papen Plan, has now dimmed. The extreme rise in raw materials last summer soon subsided. People have long known that the American panic is a volcanic eruption, and now they see this dangerous disease reappearing."

The capitalist economic panic cannot but affect the political status quo. The fantasy of the United States canceling international debts has now been shattered. The competition of mutual slaughter in the world market is extremely sharpened. Imperialist conflicts will soon turn into world wars.
