Japan's War Preparations Accelerate 229

Calling Up 100,000 Reserve Soldiers to Practice Education on New-Style Troops

According to the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun on the 22nd, the Army Ministry has already established a budget for improving the current situation and military preparedness, striving to fulfill full troop strength, implement supplementary education, and emphasize the improvement of the system and the verification of resources. The contents are as follows: (1) Improve equipment, that is, increase new-style troops (such as anti-poison education, armored vehicles, new-style artillery, radio telegraph, field warfare, meteorology, air force, air defense, balloon team, surveying team, etc.). Since April, 100,000 reserve soldiers will be gradually called up to implement emergency education. (2) Improve the system, that is (a) In order to enrich lower-level cadres, increase the number of officer cadets. From April, the number of personnel adopted at the officer school will be increased to 360, and the number of recruits at the junior school will be increased by 100. (b) Transitional measures: From April, increase the number of volunteer special sergeant majors for second lieutenants. (c) Abolish the fee-paying other-ranks officer candidate system and implement enlistment from December. (d) Newly established technical sergeant training institutions. Infantry will be trained at the Sendai, Toyohashi, and Kumamoto training schools. Cavalry and artillery will expand the Toyohashi training school. Engineers will be newly established within the engineering school. Heavy artillery will be newly established within the field heavy artillery school. Aviation and logistics will be implemented in the air force. The above-mentioned newly established education will be implemented from August. (e) Aviation junior soldiers will be trained at the Tokorozawa Flying School. (f) Increase the air force and add nine squadrons of combat bombers. Reorganize the national flying schools. (g) Expand the tank unit, enrich the Kurume First Tank Unit, and newly establish the Second Tank Unit in Narashino from August. (h) Newly established gas protection education institution. In addition to implementing some education by the Scientific Research Institute, a gas protection school will be newly established in Narashino. (i) The infantry school and the Kwantung Army will separately establish a military dog training center.

Patriotic Efforts of the People of Fujian to Resist Japan 230

Organizing Anti-Japanese Support Groups from All Walks of Life, Merchants Voluntarily Sealing Inferior Goods

Fuzhou Dispatch: Various agencies and organizations in Fujian believe that Cai Tingkai is about to lead the anti-Japanese armies of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian provinces northward. The people of the country should rise up to provide support. They have initiated the organization of the Fujian Anti-Japanese Support Association. The Pacification Headquarters, Provincial Government, Provincial Party Headquarters, Public Security Bureau, County Chamber of Commerce, Education Association, Women's Association, Money Trade Association, and 15 other agencies and organizations have been appointed as committee members. Starting from March 27th, they will begin working at the Provincial Party Headquarters, deciding to mobilize donations from April 1st to 3rd. The donation methods are divided into four types: A. Mobile: Donating to the public and passersby, undertaken by teams from various schools, each team consisting of ten people. B. Fixed: Donating to households and shops, organized by teams from various agencies, assisted by personnel from the local fire brigades. C. Surcharged: Public buses will donate 20% of their daily income, responsible by the Bus Association; Taijiang steamers will donate 20% of their daily income, responsible by the Steamer Association; rickshaws will donate two cents per vehicle per day, deducted by the rickshaw owners. D. Subscription: Letters will be sent to banks, money shops, gold shops, shipping companies, timber businesses, Su-Guang businesses, silk and cloth businesses, Jing-Cao businesses, paper businesses, pawnshops, firewood businesses, rice businesses, tea businesses, and fish businesses, asking them to subscribe donations. All donations received will be deposited in the Central Bank for unified distribution. In addition, all sectors are welcome to assist with supplies for the battlefield, such as steel helmets, sacks, straw sandals, cotton socks, medicines, and dry food, which can be sent directly to the County Chamber of Commerce for forwarding to the military. It is expected that the public will enthusiastically donate.

The people of Fuzhou have always been very strict about boycotting inferior goods. However, since the Zheng Weixin case occurred last November and the Elimination of Inferior Goods Association was dissolved, the work of boycotting goods has been relaxed, and inferior goods have been imported in a steady stream, flooding the market. Silk, Su-Guang products, seafood, hardware, and Western medicines are the most popular. Now, various merchant guilds, in view of the increasing Japanese military attacks on North China and the impending national crisis, some merchants with a sense of righteousness have suddenly awakened and convened a joint meeting of representatives of various trade guilds on March 24th. It was decided that starting from the 26th, all inferior goods stored by various guilds should be sealed up within three days and prohibited from being sold. Anyone who dares to violate this will be publicly denounced and their shop names and names will be published in the newspapers for society to deal with. Fearing that the police might misunderstand the situation and repeat the tragedy, representatives of various trade guilds visited Qiu Zhaochen, Director of the Public Security Bureau of the Provincial Capital, on the 25th to explain that this boycott movement was purely voluntary by the merchants and requested assistance. Qiu replied that within the framework of the law, he would provide full support. The various trade guilds have dispatched investigators yesterday to go to various shops in the guild to identify all inferior goods and seal them up. (March 27th)

Support Association for Anti-Japanese Army Organized in Hunan 231

Emphasizing Comfort and Assistance, Active Work After Establishment

Changsha Dispatch: The Hunan Anti-Japanese National Salvation Organization has a Supreme Cadre Conference as the highest guiding body in the province, divided into the People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, and the Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, all under the management of the Supreme Cadre and handling various academic and propaganda activities such as checking enemy capital and publicizing national salvation. Now, considering the tense military situation of the anti-Japanese war, all sectors will initiate the organization of the Hunan Support Association for the Anti-Japanese Army, with the sole task of emphasizing comfort and assistance as material support. The joint meeting of party, government, and military recently decided to allocate 400,000 yuan from the national salvation loan, with 200,000 yuan to comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers and 200,000 yuan to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army, which will be handled by the association. The association held its inaugural meeting at 3 pm on the 28th in the Flood Relief Committee, attended by over 100 representatives from all walks of life, including Huang Shiheng, Fang Kegang, Zeng Yuenong, Xie Zuyiao, Peng Guojun, etc. Hu Shuhua presided over the meeting, first passing the constitution, and then electing executive and supervisory committee members, including Hu Shuhua, Tang Gan, Miao Kunshan, Chen Suhuang, Zhou Anhan, Zeng Baosun, Chen Yangting, Fang Kegang, Xiao Enzhen, Chen Dayu, Zhou Naijia, Liu Ceheng, Peng Guojun, Chen Guanghou, and Zhou Peijun, 15 people were elected as executive committee members, and Peng Zhaohuang, Xie Guozhao, Peng Xinquan, Zheng Jiati, Ren Fuli, Pi Zongrang, Xiong Zhibai, Li Baoyi, Peng Zhuo, nine people were elected as supervisory committee members, and it was decided to start work on the 29th and actively proceed. The constitution of the association is as follows: Article 1: The purpose of this association is to assist the Anti-Japanese Army and the Northeast Volunteer Army. Article 2: This association is organized by people from all walks of life in Hunan. Article 3: The address of this association is set in the Flood Relief Committee on Lijian Street, Changsha. Article 4: This association elects 15 executive committee members to form the executive committee, whose responsibilities are as follows: (1) Collecting and handling comfort items and military supplies, and directly sending them to the front line to assist the Anti-Japanese Army; (2) Applying for the comfort funds specially raised by the joint meeting of the party, government, and military, and handling comfort matters; (3) Assisting the Northeast Volunteer Army; (4) Assisting the government in handling anti-Japanese matters. Article 5: This association appoints nine supervisory committee members to form the supervisory committee, whose responsibilities are as follows: (1) Supervising and auditing the executive committee's handling of comfort and relief matters; (2) Auditing the financial revenue and expenditure of this association. Article 6: The executive committee has five standing committee members, and the supervisory committee has three standing committee members, who are stationed in the association to handle association affairs. Article 7: The executive committee holds a regular meeting once a week, and the supervisory committee holds a regular meeting once a month. When necessary, they can convene temporary meetings. Article 8: The executive committee has general affairs, registration, procurement, storage, and escort departments, each department having one director and several staff and clerks. The supervisory committee has several staff members. Except for the clerks who receive appropriate subsidies, the rest are unpaid positions. Article 9: The funds of this association are raised by the executive and supervisory committees. Article 10: The detailed rules of this association will be determined separately. Article 11: This constitution will be submitted to the provincial party headquarters, the provincial government, and the general headquarters for approval before implementation. (March 29th)

Yao Rebellion in Guangxi Province Pacified 232

Communist Bandits Inciting Yao People to Riot, Yao People's Flags All Red, Large Army Advances and Quickly Suppresses

Nanning Dispatch: Lingchuan, Xing'an, Quanyang, Yining, and Longsheng counties mostly have Yao ethnic groups living together. In a place called Longji at the junction of Xing, Ling, and Long counties, in mid-February, Yao people gathered there numbering several thousand, building a temple to propitiate the gods, falsely claiming to support the Yao king of Quanyang to restore Yao and destroy Han. The Yao people often fantasize in their minds, believing that a Yao king will emerge from Quanyang soon. In the past, the Han and Yao people had an unusual harmony, and at the end of the year, they would give each other pork to show their amity. However, this was not done last year, and the Yao people have recently been making knives and building projects, not allowing Han people to interact with them. All Han people passing through here are inspected. Their organization is extremely strict. The Yao people are inherently ignorant and easily incited by communist bandits, so a major riot occurred, spreading to Yongfu and Xiuren areas. Therefore, although the Yining County Magistrate sent Deng Puren and Zhao Tingjian to the Yao side to enlighten them, it was all ineffective. Later, a communist bandit leader named Su fled from Jiangxi and caused trouble in Yuancun, Quan County. Of the nearby Han and Yao villagers, seven or eight out of ten were instigated by him to join. At that time, the Yao people claimed to have tens of thousands of people and posted absurd and bizarre announcements. Thus, the Yao people besieged Xing'an City, which was the beginning of the Yao people's riot. After this incident occurred, the local county governments sent telegrams asking for troops to suppress and investigate. The Fourth Group Army Headquarters ordered Division Commander Zhou to order the 57th Regiment to send three companies of troops to the area to suppress, one company to Longsheng, and the remaining two companies, led by Commander Zhang, to Xing'an area to suppress and handle according to the situation.

As for the suppression process, according to a telegram from the Xing'an County Magistrate, the reports from the 3rd, 5th, and 6th districts under the county found that the Yao people on the border of the county abandoned production and gathered for meetings, drawing knives, wearing rings, and running around wildly, with various disturbances, suggesting that someone was inciting them. The district chiefs repeatedly advised them, but they turned a deaf ear. In addition to strict prevention, further reports will be made, hoping for attention. Also, Zhang Gan, commander of the Guilin District Militia, led a team to Xingquan area on February 18th to investigate. According to Zhang's telegram, the Yao situation in various places is as follows: "Gan arrived at Mazidu and met with County Magistrate Huang, Mr. Jiang Bowen, and Deputy Commanders Qin and Tang. He immediately took the phone and listed the information obtained: (1) County Magistrate Huang reported that the Yao bandits had surrounded the Jieding Village in Jiukaitian. At noon, Yao occupied Xiandong Dayuan. The Yao bandits are taking an inch and wanting a mile. The situation is serious. (2) County Magistrate Tian reported that the Yao bandits attacked from Dengjia Village at midday. The militia is weak and retreated to Litou Market, a few miles from the county town. There were many casualties on both sides. The district commander was injured in a conflict. (3) County Magistrate Chen reported that the Yao bandits of Mujiang went to the Wuxiang Village to plunder. They were attacked and fled by the police. The situation in Wuquan, Niushi, is unknown. Lehua Long has arrived in the county town and ordered the company back to Wuquan to restrain the Yao people from joining the Tongmujiang Yao rebellion, and to persuade the Yao to wake up and not believe in rumors or be manipulated by the communist bandits. Otherwise, they will be suppressed, and explain the reason why the Yao people can be harmed by treasures. Liang has obeyed the order and is working hard to comply. (4) According to the above situation, the Yao rebellion in Xingquan has begun. It is not yet possible to predict whether the Yao of Guan will join the rebellion. It is difficult for the peace to succeed. According to County Magistrate Tian, Division Commander Zhou has added a company of troops, which will arrive in Xing by car tonight. The three parties of Xingquan and Guan are very urgent and must be suppressed with force. Gan intends to ask Division Commander Zhou to add two battalions and a machine gun company, distributed in Xingquan, to suppress them at the same time. The Yao are now rushing out of Xing, and may cross Xingcheng, intending to form a piece with the Yao in Longxingquan and the border of Hunan. If so, then increase a battalion of troops with machine guns each, and go straight to Xiangmujiang bandit nest in Quan Jianxiang, so that it can escape to Xing, and attack from both sides, and the effect can be expected. It is not easy to advance into Dengjia Village Shankou, but Jianxiang is easy to attack." Also, the Xing'an County Magistrate telegraphed, saying that the Yao bandits in Dengjia Village, numbering more than 2,000, rushed fiercely at our police, and many police were killed or injured. The six soldiers left by Commander Zhang were also killed or injured. Now the guns and bullets are lacking, and there is no way to resist. They can only temporarily retreat to Moyuan Village, five miles from the city. The bandits are still approaching. Please send a large team of cars to rescue them.

Chen En yuan, deputy division commander of the 19th Division, rushed to Xingquan to suppress the rebellion after receiving urgent telegrams from various parties, and first sent four companies of soldiers, one company of mortars, and two companies of machine guns, to Xinglong on the 22nd. The Yao bandits were a motley crowd, lacking in equipment, and upon hearing that Chen had led a large army to suppress them, they knew they could not resist, so they fled back to their lair in a panic. Chen is now implementing both suppression and pacification, sending troops to suppress while also announcing the government's good intentions to engage in pacification. At that time, some Yao people had already come to their senses and were not incited by the bandits, willing to surrender their weapons. The Yao crowd gradually disintegrated. The 19th Division headquarters sent troops to suppress them, achieving a great victory. The Yao bandits suffered countless casualties. It was heard that the Dongshan Yao in the Quan area were searched and suppressed by government troops, and their main force was attacked and dispersed. Thus, the Yao rebellion was pacified.

Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi, seeing that the Yao rebellion was pacified, telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Council to report, saying, "The Yao people in Quan County, Xing'an, Quanyang, Yining, Longsheng, and Lingchuan counties in Guilin have recently been gathering to rebel in various places under the pretext of building temples and carrying gods. Repeatedly sending personnel to pacify them was ineffective. Recently, the Yao people in various places have gathered about four or five million people. The flags and symbols are all red. The weapons include knives, spears, powder guns, and rifles and pistols. They are using 'Revive Yao and Destroy Han' as their slogan, threatening and luring people wherever they go, absorbing strong men, or carrying out massacres. The Yao on the borders of Hunan and Guizhou are rising up in response, and the situation is very turbulent. It has been confirmed that there are important communist party members presiding over it. Considering the communist party's conspiracy to harm Guilin, using the Yao people to provoke fighting between Han and Yao people as a starting point, the false CCP member Wei Baqun has poisoned Dongfeng for many years with the slogan of 'Keeping Yao and Killing Tu'. Fortunately, he was killed last year. This time, the party is using the same method to instigate the Yao people in various places in Guizhou, Hunan, and Guangxi to launch a large-scale riot, attempting to disrupt the border between Hunan and Guangxi. We should extinguish it as soon as possible to avoid great trouble. We have sent Army Commander Liao to supervise five regiments of troops and the Guilin District Militia to be responsible for the suppression. Now we have broken several bandit nests. The remaining small groups have also been repeatedly defeated by the army. In addition to ordering the troops to collect weapons, eliminate the ringleaders, and disband the coerced from the defeated bandits, we will properly arrange the aftermath to ensure that the case is concluded as soon as possible, and we will submit the details in a separate document. We respectfully report for your review, and hope you will check. Li Zongren Bai Chongxi report."

Chen Guangfu Telegrams Paris 233

Reasons for Suspending Participation in the International Chamber of Commerce

The 7th International Chamber of Commerce Congress will be held in Vienna on the 29th of next month. Chen Guangfu and Guo Bingwen, the chairman and vice-chairman of the Chinese National Committee, respectively, believed that under the current urgent national crisis, attendees would be unwilling to participate, so it was decided to suspend attendance at this congress. Chairman Chen also telegraphed the Paris General Chamber of Commerce on the way to Changsha, Hunan, stating the reasons for his absence.

Liao Chengzhi Released on Bail Last Night 234

Still Subject to Legal Trial

Liao Chengzhi, son of martyr Liao Zhongkai, was arrested by the Zhabei Police on the 28th of last month for suspected communism and sent to the Higher Second Branch Court. After two interrogations, he was transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau along with the evidence yesterday. Liao's mother, He Xiangning, and CCP member Liu Yazi bailed him out at midnight yesterday. The details are as follows:

(Released on Bail Last Night) After the Higher Second Branch Court ruled yesterday to transfer Liao Chengzhi to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, he was taken back to the Public Security Bureau for detention by Inspector Lu of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday evening. Liao's mother, He Xiangning, has been bedridden recently due to her concern for her son. She struggled to get up and was helped downstairs upon learning that her son had been transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. She went to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau with CCP member Liu Yazi and lawyer Wu Kaisheng to visit her son. The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau then agreed to release him on bail. Liu Yazi and He Xiangning provided bail. By about 11 pm, all the procedures were completed, and Liao Chengzhi was released and returned to his residence to rest with his mother.

(He Xiangning's Statement) He Xiangning told the Central News Agency reporter this morning that since her son Chengzhi was arrested, the military and political authorities, considering the friendship of her late husband Liao Zhongkai, have been running around to rescue him and secure his release on bail. She expressed her gratitude. However, her late husband Liao Zhongkai always held the spirit of universal love. She deeply hoped that the military and political authorities would, considering Liao's past friendship, rescue the political prisoners of the country with the spirit of rescuing Liao's descendants, so that they could work together to overcome national difficulties and save China from crisis.

(Liao Chengzhi's Statement) He then introduced her son Liao Chengzhi to meet the reporter. Liao recounted the process of his arrest, saying, "I have only returned to China from Germany for over a month. On the 28th of last month, I was ordered by my mother to go to No. 9 Wufu Lane, Shanxi Road, to meet tea merchant Ouyang Chun to order tea leaves to be transported to the Northeast to comfort the soldiers on the front line. However, as soon as I entered, Ouyang was not there, and I was arrested by the inspectors of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and detained in the Zhabei Police. It was not until yesterday that I was transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. I was released last night after Mr. Liu Yazi and my mother bailed me out. As for myself, I have always not known what communism is, and I have no political affiliations."

(Trial According to Law) According to a responsible spokesperson of the municipal government, regarding the Liao Chengzhi case, because Liao's mother, He Xiangning, was concerned about her son and bedridden, she was allowed to post bail and be summoned at any time. Yesterday, Liu and He were responsible for posting bail. As for this case, Liao Chengzhi is only suspected, so he will still be transferred to the responsible authorities for trial according to law to clarify the truth.

Police Find Communist Propaganda Cloth 235

Containing More Than 161,000 Words, But Chen Shuying Insists It Is Not Hers

The "North-China Daily News" reports that the Special Branch of the Shanghai Municipal Police recently cracked a communist party organization in the Settlement and discovered a large number of hidden documents. After applying chemicals, the handwriting was revealed. It appears to be the complete documents of the General Bureau of the Chinese Communist Party, i.e., the National General Labor Union. The organization was located upstairs in a cigarette paper shop at No. 290 Mei Bai Ge Road. The occupants were Chen Guang and his wife, and Chen's younger sister, Shuying. Chen Guang and his wife have escaped, so only Chen Shuying was captured. At the time of the arrest, detectives found many white willow cloth and white paper in her room. Afterwards, they applied chemicals to a handkerchief found in the room and discovered the principles of communist propaganda in the Kuomintang army written in Chinese. Then they took several pieces of white willow cloth and applied the same chemical experiment, and all had handwriting. Among them were communist leaflets, notices, and books, and instructions on how to fire machine guns and throw bombs in the sky. There were 43 pieces of cloth, about 27 inches wide and 43 feet long. It is estimated that each foot has 3,750 characters, so 43 feet have more than 161,250 characters. The end of each section is written with the type of content. Except for a few leaflets on the Shanghai Memorial Day and the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the rest are records of the Communist Party's activities in Manchuria, Hunan, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hebei, Fujian, Qin, and Henan provinces. In addition, 38 copies of "Red Flag Weekly" were seized, the earliest of which was published in December 1931, and the most recent of which was published on March 8 of this year. It is said that the cloth contains a true record of the work of the National General Labor Union in the past two years. Also found in the room were a large number of white paper and light yellow paper, and many blank exercise books, all of which are thought to have handwriting. Chen Shuying, who was arrested, speaks Russian and insists that the items seized by the detectives were stored by her father's friend, surnamed Yu.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Establishes Donation Collection Office for Northeast Relief 237

Based on the Requests of More Than 70 Associations

Entrusting Banks and Money Shops to Collect Donations

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce decided at its 32nd Standing Committee meeting yesterday to establish an office for raising donations to aid the Northeast, appointing Luo Qinghua as the director of the office, and appointing banks and money shops as collection points. At the same time, it issued a declaration, the text of which is as follows: "Since the Northeast has fallen and the volunteer army is fighting bloody battles in the remote areas, the Chamber has taken the initiative to organize a Northeast Refugee Relief Association in conjunction with all sectors. Now, according to the request of more than 70 associations such as silk-rayon weaving industry, this monthly donation is actually made by the business community. In order to rectify the name and define the responsibility, and to arouse the business community's sense of self-awareness and responsibility, it is appropriate to take sole responsibility and eliminate dependence. This is in line with the ancient saying of 'not shirking responsibility' and achieving the practical effect of 'turning stubbornness into integrity.' It is proposed that the Chamber form a Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Donation Raising Committee for National Salvation, etc." The Joint Executive and Supervisory Committee referred it to the 32nd Standing Committee meeting for discussion. According to the requests of various industries, it issued a declaration and established the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Donation Raising Office for Northeast Relief in the Chamber, appointing Committee Member Luo Qinghua as the director of the office, and designated the Bank of China, the Salt Industry Bank, the Silk Industry Bank, the Tongchun Money Shop, the Hengxun Money Shop, the Siming Savings Society, and the Chamber's Finance Section as collection points. From now on, there will be a dedicated person in charge. All merchants should save money and food and help the country in difficulty, striving to be pioneers in all walks of life. This is a special declaration. (New Voice)

US Flagship Houston Arrives in Shanghai Today from the South 238

The flagship of the US Asiatic Fleet, the Houston, arrived in Shanghai today from the south and is scheduled to berth in the Huangpu River for two months, then sail to Qingdao for five or six weeks, and then to Yantai for summer exercises, or possibly to Qinhuangdao along the way. The ship is a 10,000-ton cruiser, carrying 35 officers, about 600 sailors, equipped with eight-inch guns, and carrying four seaplanes. When it berths in Shanghai, Admiral Datner, Commander of the US Asiatic Fleet, and 15 staff officers will work on the ship.

Labor Dispute in Nanyang: Labor Representatives Petition Party and Government Again 241

Union Petitions for Withdrawal of Detectives, Requests Mediation for Early Resumption of Work

Regarding the dispute at the Nanyang Tobacco Company, because the company's detectives have not yet withdrawn, and eleven staff members of the office are afraid of being arrested by the factory, they have not yet returned to the factory to resume work. This morning at 11:00 AM, the Nanyang office again petitioned the Party and government. The Fourth District Cigarette Industry Union separately submitted a petition to the Party and government for an early mediation. The details are recorded below:

Staff Petitions: The Nanyang office of the Fourth District Cigarette Industry Union, because the company's detectives have not yet withdrawn and they fear being arrested again if they resume work, specifically dispatched representatives Xiao Guangde, Zhang Hua, Wu Shiyuan, Yu Xingqing, Xu Zhubao, Weng Lin, Zhou Jian, Xu Ronggen, Wang Yunsheng and others this morning at 11:00 AM to petition the Party and government, requesting early mediation and asking them to order the police station to withdraw the detectives. The Social Bureau was met by mediation director Wang Xianqing, who expressed that the Bureau had already reported this to the Municipal Government and was awaiting the Municipal Government's notification to the police station to handle it. They then went to the Municipal Party Headquarters to submit the same petition, where they were met by Zhang Sheng, the chief of the Civil Training Section, who stated that the proposed prerequisites were still under consideration and promised to coordinate with the Social Bureau to schedule a mediation.

Union Submission: The Fourth District Cigarette Industry Union submitted a document to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Bureau yesterday, stating that it was a petitioning matter. The Nanyang office of the Union, in order to request the signing of labor-capital prerequisites, unwillingly experienced a strike on the 20th of last month. The factory falsely reported to the police station, arresting five staff members and workers from the office and transferring them to the court. Staff member Wu Shiyuan and worker Li Jingfa were tried and released on bail last Tuesday. The rest are still in custody, with the trial rescheduled. The factory's behavior of wanting to arrest the staff and conduct security measures has been negotiated by the union and bureau who have jointly sent personnel, who agreed to withdraw it, but this has not yet been implemented. It is only appropriate to submit a document to once again petition your union and bureau to quickly transfer a notification to the police station, withdraw the armed detectives from the factory, and also request a prompt mediation to maintain the livelihood of the workers. This would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully submitted.

Yoshizawa Inspects Zhabei War Zone 242

Also Visits Japanese Cemetery to Mourn Fallen Soldiers

Former Japanese Ambassador to China, Yoshizawa Kenkichi, accompanied by a group of three including Member of the House of Peers, Iwaki, and Member of the Diet, Hashimoto, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. They immediately attended a banquet hosted by the Japanese community and Japanese military and political authorities at the Rokusan-tei on Peng Road. That night, they stayed at the Astor House Hotel. In order to understand the situation in the aftermath of the January 28th Shanghai Incident, Yoshizawa and his party, along with Counselor Arino from the embassy, Consul General Ishii Jutaro, Commander of the Japanese Naval Landing Force Sugisaka, and others, took three cars to inspect the Zhabei area this morning at 8:30 AM. The Japanese side notified our military and political authorities in advance, so Jin Gong, the district chief of the Fifth District of the Municipal Police Bureau, and Patrol Officer Cao, and others guided them. After the inspection, Yoshizawa and his party went directly to the Japanese cemetery at Baziqiao to mourn the fallen soldiers and lay wreaths. They returned to the Astor House Hotel at 10:10 AM.

Man and Woman Walking Side by Side 243

Suddenly Spotted by Chief Inspector Quan, Identified as Old Man Xu San

Quan Lin, Chief Inspector of the Anti-Bandit Command on the Su Song Waterways, was passing through Rehe Road yesterday afternoon when he saw a middle-aged man from Anhui Province walking side by side with a young woman from Jiangbei. Chief Inspector Quan believed the man was the notorious Old Man Xu San, who was a wanted bandit. He had committed crimes such as kidnapping for ransom and armed robbery in Suzhou in August of last year. Three of his accomplices had been arrested in Suzhou, and Xu was on a wanted list issued by the Anti-Bandit Commander Xu Ke. He then reported to No. 787 Chinese police officer, who arrested the man and woman together and took them to the police station. Under questioning by the police chief, the man denied being Old Man Xu San, and claimed his name was Yang Baohua. The young woman claimed to be Yang Chenshi, Baohua's wife, and said that the couple had come to Shanghai from Zhenjiang just half a month ago and were renting a place at 457 Kaifeng Road and were currently looking for work, and had no history of crime. However, Chief Inspector Quan insisted that the man's surname was indeed the wanted bandit Xu, and since the woman was the bandit's wife, she was also an accomplice. He presented the secret order given to him by the commander as proof. The police chief then ordered the man and woman to be detained separately and sent to the First Special District Local Court this morning. Judge Qian Wenji conducted a preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, explained the situation and stated that if the inspector wanted to request a transfer, he should be ordered to provide substantial evidence and the command should have a formal transfer document before the transfer could be approved. Judge Qian immediately instructed Quan Lin to do so in accordance with these two points, and ordered the man and woman to be detained separately, rescheduling the hearing for a later date.

American Soldiers Throw Eggs at Japanese Soldiers 244

The Shanghai Times reports that last night, a truck full of armed Japanese naval landing forces was driving on Nanjing Road when three American sailors suddenly threw several eggs at them, hitting two Japanese soldiers in the face. Another seven uniforms were stained. The Japanese soldiers were furious and stopped the truck to chase after the egg throwers, but the three Americans had already achieved their purpose and fled far away.

New Rules for Handling Electricity Theft 245

Effective from April 1st

The Rules for Electricity Business Operators Inspecting Electricity Theft and Recovering Electricity Fees, promulgated by the Construction Committee in April of the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930), have been in effect for over two years. After reviewing the situation, it was deemed necessary to amend and supplement them. Therefore, in October of last year, a draft of the Rules for Electricity Business Operators Handling Electricity Theft was re-drafted, and opinions were widely solicited from relevant agencies and experts from various locations. It was compiled, reviewed, and revised into sixteen articles. This new regulation has been decided and promulgated by the Construction Committee at a meeting on January 6th of this year and is scheduled to take effect from April 1st, according to the New Life News Agency.
